Zhang Xueliang Will Reside in Beiping

▲ Reorganization of Political System in the Three Eastern Provinces Also Imminent

(Shenyang Dispatch) Urged by the Central Government, Zhang Xueliang assumed the position of Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force on the 9th. Henceforth, the Northeast will further demonstrate its support for the Central Government. The Central Government appointed Zhang to the position to reward him for his contributions to the Party and the nation and to task him with managing the aftermath in the North. Upon assuming office, Zhang decided in a recent cadre meeting that he would depart for Beiping within days to take up residence. The location for his Deputy Commander-in-Chief's headquarters has also been designated in Beiping. Special commissioners have been dispatched to prepare the official residence. It is also planned to invite Commander-in-Chief Chiang to meet in Beiping to discuss all matters. Zhang's departure for Beiping is scheduled to take place within ten days. The Third Army, commanded by Hu Yukun, is being organized to accompany him into the pass, or at least a portion of the army. After Zhang Xueliang leaves Shenyang, the duties of the Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast Border Defense will be temporarily assumed by Zhang Zuoxiang. Concurrently, Wan Fulin, Chairman of Heilongjiang Province, Tang Yulin, Chairman of Rehe Province, and Zhang Jinghui, Chief Executive of the Harbin Special District, will also leave Shenyang to return to their original posts. Thus, the Northeast's alignment with the Central Government can be said to have reached a certain stage under the goal of supporting the central government. Zhang Qun, the Special Mayor of Shanghai, who previously bore a significant mission, departed for Dalian on the 11th, considering his mission to be fulfilled, and will return to Nanjing by sea to report on his duties. Wu Tiecheng, also scheduled to go west on the 12th to handle party affairs in Beiping. All liaison matters between the Central Government and the Northeast will be handled by Fang Benren.

Another report indicates that the allegiance of the Northeast to the Central Government was pledged at the end of last year. Due to various reasons, the establishment of positions such as the Northeast Political Affairs Committee, the Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast Border Defense, and the Deputy Commander in Jilin were temporary measures, seemingly inconsistent with the organization and systems stipulated by the National Government. It is heard that Zhang Xueliang, before assuming the position of Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, discussed these matters several times with Zhang Zuoxiang, Wan Fulin, and Tang Yulin. Since the Northeast and the National Government are now moving towards unity, it is proposed to abolish the Political Affairs Committee and implement separate military and civil governance in each province, with complete obedience to the Central Government. Upon the Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force assuming office, the position of Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast Border Defense will be offered to Zhang Zuoxiang, but Zhang Zuoxiang has repeatedly declined the offer. If this materializes, Zhang's position as Deputy Commander in Jilin will be given to Zhang Jinghui, the Chief Executive of the Harbin Special District, and Xi Qia will be promoted to Chief Executive of the Special District. Regarding the issue of separate military and civil governance, a certain important figure has recommended Cheng Yun as the Chairman of Jilin Province and Rong Hou as the Chairman of Heilongjiang Province. Tang Yulin, the Chairman of Rehe, will be appointed as the Commander of the Garrison in Rehe and Suiyuan. An announcement is expected soon, as the First and Second Armies of the Northeast have already entered the Pingjin area and are advancing along the Pinghan and Pingsui lines. In the future, Suiyuan will also fall under the Northeast's sphere of influence. Whether the above points have been fully discussed and agreed upon or whether there will be other changes in the future remains to be seen. This is recorded for observation. (11th)

Recent Important News in Diplomatic Circles

▲ Sino-British Negotiations: During his visit to Nanjing, the British Minister Sir Miles Lampson resolved several important pending issues between China and Britain. The British Concession in Xiamen has been returned, Weihaiwei has been handed over to China, and the Boxer Indemnity refund agreement has been signed. These are all important developments in Sino-British relations.

The British Concession in Xiamen did not have clear regulations. Its origin lies in Article 2 of the Sino-British Treaty of Daoguang 22 (July), which stipulated that British people were permitted to reside, trade, and conduct business in Xiamen with their families. Article 7 of the Sino-British Supplementary Treaty of Commerce of Daoguang 23 (August) stipulated that British people were permitted to lease houses and land in Xiamen, with the British Consul notifying the local authorities for registration. In Daoguang 24 (August), the local officials of Xiamen and the British reached an agreement to designate the South Training Ground and the Naval Drill Ground in Xiamen as the British Concession. This was the origin of the British Concession in Xiamen. These two areas were quite far from the Xiamen docks, which was inconvenient for British businesses, so an additional section was leased. The total area was approximately 90 zhang in length. Its nature can only be described as leased land and not a concession. The organization of the Xiamen Concession Municipal Council began in Guangxu 3 (1877). Its scale was extremely small and could not be compared to those in Hankou, Jiujiang, and Zhenjiang. After the May Thirtieth Movement in the Republic of China 14 (1925), the British Consulate in Xiamen, in order to protect British residents, accepted the Chinese side's proposal to abolish the Municipal Council police. All administrative rights within the concession were completely handed over to the Chinese police. Thereafter, the so-called British Concession existed only in name. Therefore, the procedure for the current return was simple. Once the deed was completed, it could be said that the return was realized.

The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity exchange of notes was signed on September 22. It stipulated that the British government, after the necessary legislation was passed by the Parliament, would return the full amount of the Boxer Indemnity due from December 1, 1922, to the Chinese government for management. The Chinese government would use the majority of the returned funds to establish a foundation for the reorganization and construction of railways and invest in other Chinese productive enterprises as loans, subject to interest payments. It also stipulated the organization of a purchasing committee to buy materials in England for Chinese railway construction. In addition, it was determined that 265,000 pounds would be allocated to the University of Hong Kong for the education of Chinese students, and 200,000 pounds would be allocated to the London China Universities Committee for inviting famous Chinese figures to lecture in England and promote cultural exchange between China and Britain. The content of the exchange of notes is roughly as described above. The original text will be published soon. The handover of Weihaiwei has been completed, so further details are not repeated here.

▲ Sino-Russian Negotiations: The formal Sino-Russian conference officially commenced on the 11th of this month. The scope of this conference is broader than previous discussions. In addition to the issue of the Chinese Eastern Railway, issues such as transportation and commerce are also on the agenda. The Chinese side advocates discussing the Chinese Eastern Railway issue first. After a resolution is reached, other issues will be discussed. The Central Government will dispatch four additional experts to Moscow to assist in the proceedings.

▲ Sino-Japanese Telecommunications Conference: The Sino-Japanese Telecommunications Conference has only convened twice since its opening on September 17. The third meeting was originally scheduled for October 1, but it was postponed because the Japanese side wanted to consider the Chinese proposals in detail. However, it is expected to convene soon and continue the discussions. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has also notified the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires that the Qingdao-Sasebo submarine cable agreement will expire at the end of this year and that China will take back and manage it independently. The Ministry has requested that the Japanese Ministry of Communications be notified to hand it over by the deadline. Furthermore, the Ministry has also notified the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires to notify the Datong and Dabeij submarine cable companies that their contracts will be cancelled at the end of this year and that foreigners will never be allowed to enjoy submarine cable landing rights in China.

▲ Treaty Negotiations: Several countries are currently involved in treaty negotiations. These are described separately below: (A) Sino-Siamese: There are a large number of overseas Chinese and Chinese merchants in Siam. Due to the lack of treaty relations between China and Siam, it is impossible to protect the overseas Chinese in Siam, causing considerable hardship to the diaspora. Since the establishment of the National Government, it has repeatedly proposed treaty negotiations to the Siamese government, but without satisfactory results. Recently, during a meeting of the League of Nations, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs took advantage of the opportunity to instruct the Chinese Minister Wu to propose Sino-Siamese treaty negotiations to the Siamese representative. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently received a telegram from Minister Wu stating that the Siamese representative has agreed to propose the negotiation of a Sino-Siamese treaty to his government upon his return to Siam. (B) Sino-Panamanian: The Sino-Panamanian commercial treaty is being negotiated by the Chinese Chargé d'Affaires in Panama, Li Shizhong, and the Panamanian government. Once a draft treaty is agreed upon, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will request the National Government to issue full powers for signing. (C) Sino-Czechoslovakian: The Sino-Czechoslovakian Treaty of Amity and Commerce was signed in Nanjing on February 13 of this year. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently received a letter from the Czech representative stating that the Sino-Czechoslovakian commercial treaty was formally ratified by the Czech President on September 27. The ratification documents will be personally delivered by the newly appointed Chargé d'Affaires, Dr. Rafael. The Ministry has replied, expressing the hope that Representative Rafael will come to China as soon as possible to exchange ratification documents with the Ministry so that the treaty can take effect as soon as possible. (D) Sino-Peruvian: The Sino-Peruvian treaty is being negotiated by the Chinese Chargé d'Affaires in Peru, Wei Zijing, and the Peruvian government. However, there is still no agreement on the treatment of overseas Chinese in Peru, which has delayed the formation of a draft treaty. Due to the recent coup in Peru, there will be a temporary halt. However, consultations will resume with the new government soon.

▲ Establishment of Consulates: The establishment of consulates can also be described in several points: (A) Annam: The Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently received telegrams from various groups in Annam urging the establishment of a consulate. The Sino-French Vietnam commercial treaty has not yet been ratified by the governments of both countries. Once the ratification documents are exchanged, consuls will be appointed to Annam. (B) Dili: The Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that there is a need to establish a consulate in Portuguese Dili due to the large number of overseas Chinese there. It has recently telegraphed the Chinese Minister to Portugal, Wang Tingzhang, instructing him to seek the Portuguese government's consent. (C) Poland: After the signing of the Sino-Polish commercial treaty and protocol, there are no major issues between the two countries. China has long since ratified the commercial treaty, but the protocol has not yet been ratified, so it has not yet been implemented. The Polish parliament has now been dissolved. The Polish government has recognized the treaty, so the protocol can be implemented once it is ratified by the Chinese Legislative Yuan. It is also planned to exchange ambassadors and consuls.

▲ Protection of Overseas Chinese: Regarding the increase in entry tax by the Dutch East Indies, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has repeatedly protested. According to a report from the Chinese embassy in the Netherlands, the Council of the Dutch East Indies, in order to supplement the budget, will increase the entry tax from 100 guilders to 150 guilders, effective January 1 of next year. This matter has been submitted by the Council to the Dutch government for review. The Dutch Colonial Office has now sent it back to the Council for further discussion. A final decision has not been made. A protest has been lodged with the Dutch government, requesting that it earnestly cancel this proposal in order to preserve the friendship between the two countries. In addition, the Dutch East Indies government also proposes to increase the stamp tax on residence permits. This matter has also been protested to the Dutch government. Recently, the Dutch East Indies has also imposed various restrictions and guarantees on incoming overseas Chinese. If these are implemented, travelers to the Dutch East Indies will inevitably waste time and money. This is not the way to treat people from friendly nations. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has instructed the Chinese Chargé d'Affaires in the Netherlands to lodge a serious protest with the Dutch government.

Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai Arrive in Hankou

(Hankou Express Dispatch) Jiang Guangnai, Commander-in-Chief of the Nineteenth Route Army and Commander of the Sixtieth Division, and Cai Tingkai, Commander of the Eighteenth Army and Commander of the Sixty-first Division, arrived in Hankou at 11:00 AM on the 16th aboard a special train on the Pinghan Railway. A reporter rushed to interview them and had a brief conversation, the main points of which are as follows: (Reporter) Commander-in-Chief Jiang and Commander Cai, how many people accompanied you on this trip from Xuchang to Hankou? (Jiang) We departed from Xuchang the day before yesterday and arrived in Hankou today. The only companion is Comrade Lin Yizhong, the representative of the comfort delegation dispatched by Commander-in-Chief Chen Jitang of the Eighth Route Army, besides a few guards. (Reporter) According to Chief He of the General Headquarters, your troops have been transferred to Hankou to assist in suppressing the Communist bandits in Hubei. Where are your troops currently concentrated, and when will they depart for Hubei? (Jiang) After receiving the order to transfer to Hubei, our division concentrated in Xuchang and prepared to begin transportation on the 18th. However, there is a shortage of vehicles on the Pinghan Railway, so it will be difficult to arrive completely at once. (Reporter) Commander-in-Chief and Commander Cai, you have participated in the campaign against the rebels, traversed thousands of miles, and contributed greatly. We would like to hear about your past achievements. (Jiang) It is the duty of revolutionary soldiers to suppress rebellion and defend the Party and the nation. There is no merit to speak of. However, after our troops eliminated Zhang Guitang in Hunan, we joined the battles on the Longhai and Jinpu lines. The fighting was fierce beyond compare. Fortunately, thanks to the virtue of the Commander-in-Chief and the efforts of all the officers and soldiers, we recovered Jinan, causing the rebel forces of Yan and Feng to collapse. Subsequently, our troops were ordered to participate in the battles on the Pinghan Line. At that time, Feng's rebel troops, with six divisions of Liang Guanying, Zhang Weixi, Tian Jinkai, Liu Ruming, and others, stubbornly resisted between Xuchang and Zhengzhou. Our troops' line was northwest of Xuchang. After our troops fought hard and surrounded them, the rebel troops fled to the northwest of Xuchang, where they were intercepted by our troops. In that battle, more than 50,000 to 60,000 people were disarmed. Later, the rebel troops fled to the southeast of Xuchang and were intercepted by Gu Zhutong's Eighth Column and Jiang Dingwen's Ninth Column, and many were disarmed. By this point, Feng's main force had been almost completely lost. (Reporter) When will the fighting on the front lines be completely over? Where will the pursuit of Feng's fleeing troops continue? (Jiang) The military campaign against the rebels should be over soon. The pursuit of the remnants of Feng's rebels is planned to continue to Shaanxi and Gansu to save the people of the Northwest. (Reporter) What is the recent situation of the Gui troops? (Jiang) The Gui rebel troops have suffered repeated heavy blows and only have a small area left. Their firearms are no more than a few thousand, so there is definitely no problem. (Reporter) Commander-in-Chief and Commander Cai, will you stay in Hankou for a long time or will you go elsewhere? (Jiang) We plan to stay in Hankou for two or three days and then fly to Nanjing. Whether we return to Guangdong or return to Hankou after that will be decided after meeting with the Commander-in-Chief. Where the headquarters and division headquarters will be located in the future must also be requested from the Commander-in-Chief. At this point, the reporter took his leave. (October 16)

Jiaozhou Naval and Army Forces Engage Bandits

▲ Wang Ziming's Band Completely Eliminated

▲ Over 200 Killed, Over 100 Captured

(Qingdao Dispatch) Zhan Shutang, the commander of the 73rd division, was ordered to suppress bandits in Jiaozhou. After arriving, Commander Zhan along with the county magistrate of Jiaoxian, Xie Caizhang led the troops south and moved their headquarters to Wangtai town. At the same time, the Qingdao based Navy also sent the Jiangli warship carrying Marines to Haixi to assist in the battle and prevent the bandits from fleeing east. The order to attack was given on the 11th, surrounding about 1,000 bandits led by Wang Ziming in Shuicheng and Xuejialing, located about 35 li south of Wangtai. A fierce battle ensued, resulting in over 200 bandits killed on the spot, including a bandit deputy commander and five regimental commanders. Over 100 bandits were captured, and four mortars and dozens of Mauser pistols were seized. The remaining hundreds of bandits broke through the encirclement and fled to Xiaomawan in the eastern countryside, where they ransacked supplies. The county government urgently dispatched the militia of the Hanxin District to intercept them. At that time, Zhang Maode, the commander of the 218th Brigade, had already led his troops to pursue. On the evening of the 12th, the bandits fled again to Yangjiatun, only 20 li away from the county seat. Commander Zhan, upon receiving the report, dispatched a large force on the 13th to encircle and suppress them. At the same time, the militias from the western countryside of Jimo and the southern countryside of Pingdu also rushed to assist. Attacked from both sides, the bandit forces could not withstand the pressure and scattered and fled. The bandit gang of Wang Ziming was completely eliminated at this point. The remaining bandits are still being eliminated by the county government, which has mobilized the militias from various townships to join the suppression effort. Commander Zhan and County Magistrate Xie triumphantly returned to the city on the 12th. On the 13th, over 30 captured bandits were executed as a warning. The people of the entire county held a celebration rally on the morning of the 14th to welcome the returning soldiers. Commander Zhan and County Magistrate Xie both gave speeches. Now that the major threat has been eliminated, Commander Zhan does not need to stay in Jiaoxian for long. He led his troops back to Weixian on the 15th to resume defensive duties. The Marines also returned to Qingdao yesterday to report the bandit suppression operations to the Naval Headquarters. (October 15)

Symington's Letter to Zhang Xueliang

▲ Intent on Preserving His Position

▲ Zhang Xueliang Refuses Sternly

The Kuomintang News Agency reports that Symington, who previously forcibly occupied the Tianjin Customs and resisted the Central Government, sent a letter to Zhang Xueliang in Shenyang, thinking to use 2 million yuan in Tianjin Customs revenue as the price to secure his position. He was sternly refused by Zhang. The full text of Symington's plea for assistance is recorded below: "To General Zhang, I hereby submit this letter to inform you of the details of the Tianjin Customs, including all immediately available tax revenue and the amounts that can be remitted each month. Only Your Excellency can find a way to maintain the position of Symington and his current colleagues. If you are willing to appoint Symington as the Commissioner of the Tianjin Customs, the tens of thousands of yuan in surplus tax revenue can be remitted immediately. In my humble opinion, Your Excellency should follow the old example of the Shanxi authorities and grant Symington the titles of Commissioner of the Tianjin Customs and Advisor. Then, I can directly sign checks and present them to Your Excellency. In addition to the accumulated cash revenue, there are still 640,000 taels of Haikwan silver deposited in the Bank of Communications, which was previously handed over. The Shanxi authorities have repeatedly demanded the withdrawal of this amount, but I have refused. Furthermore, there are 350,000 yuan in Boxer Indemnity from Russia for the month of September. Taiyuan has also telegraphed, urging the remittance of this amount within a week, but I have not complied. Furthermore, according to the national cigarette tax rate in China, it is originally 33%. Recently, the Shanxi authorities raised the cigarette tax in Hebei to 50%. As a result, the British-American Tobacco factory in Tianjin was forced to shut down. If Your Excellency can restore the original tax rate, then I can have the British-American Tobacco company immediately pay 500,000 to 600,000 yuan in stamp tax. In summary, raising over 2 million yuan in cash is within my capabilities. In addition, the monthly tax revenue is also over 1 million yuan. Apart from the financial support, if Your Excellency appoints me as the Tianjin Customs Commissioner, then I will be a man of Your Excellency and can also increase Your Excellency's influence considerably. Tianjin Customs is the second largest customs in China, with as many as 458 employees. The annual revenue is over 26 million yuan. Since I took over, I have recruited talent from all over the country and implemented major reforms, making it a true Chinese customs. This can also be called a major progress in your country. All the old malpractices have been eliminated without a trace, and the entire customs has been transformed. This is a well-known fact. Now, the old staff of Tianjin Customs are thinking of returning to their old positions, wanting to destroy the work I have painstakingly managed, and have announced that they will expel me tomorrow (Monday). I have decided to resist them with all my might. Recently, a friend came from outside the customs and told me everything, so I wrote this hastily. I have always been loyal to the late General Zhang Zuolin for a long time. After his death, I worked hard to expose the truth of his assassination to the world. Now that I am in a critical situation, I dare to beg for Your Excellency's assistance. The Nanjing authorities have repeatedly threatened me. If their threats materialize, then my reputation will be ruined from now on. If I am accepted, then I will do my best to repay Your Excellency and the entire Liaoning province. I beg for a secret instruction. If I am favored with an appointment, then the world will know that I have the most important figures in China as my backing, and my position can be secured from then on. I originally intended to explain everything in person, but the situation in the customs is serious, and I dare not overstep my bounds. I humbly submit this letter with a detailed account, wishing you good health, Symington, September 21st."

Liaoning Province National Day Commemoration Ceremony

(Shenyang Dispatch) The Double Tenth National Day Commemoration Ceremony was held in the auditorium of the Provincial Government. The key figures who participated included Central Government representatives Zhang Qun, Wu Tiecheng, and Fang Benren, as well as Zhang Zuoxiang, Wan Fulin, Tang Yulin, Zhang Jinghui, Hu Ruoyu, consuls from Britain, the United States, Japan, Germany, France, and Russia stationed in Shenyang, leaders of the Border Defense Commander's Office, the Provincial Government, various civil and military agencies, and representatives of guests, totaling over 400 people. They gathered together at 10:00 AM, arriving one after another. The order of the ceremony was as follows: (1) Gathering at the venue at 10:00 AM; (2) Ringing the bell to commence the ceremony at 10:30 AM; (3) Playing music; (4) Removing hats and standing in silence; (5) Bowing three times to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen; (6) Music stops; (7) The Chairman reads the last will and testament of Dr. Sun Yat-sen; (8) Silent mourning for three minutes; (9) Report; (10) Singing the national anthem; (11) Chanting "Long live the Republic of China" three times; (12) Ceremony concludes, photo session, and dismissal.

After holding the celebration at the Provincial Government, Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang went to the Beida Camp at 1:00 PM to hold a military parade. All arrangements have been seen in yesterday's newspaper. This parade was the first ceremonial event after Zhang assumed the post of Deputy Commander-in-Chief. Both Chinese and foreign people wanted to witness its grandeur. Observers flocked to the scene endlessly. From the city to the Beida Camp parade ground, people and horses came and went like weaving. Various schools and organizations gathered around the parade ground, overcrowded and chaotic. Numerous police and guards were stationed along the way to maintain strict security. In the venue, the four characters "Promote Our Military Might" were inscribed in front of the lounge for Deputy Commander Zhang, senior officials, and Chinese and foreign guests, appearing splendid and solemn. National Government representatives Zhang Qun, Wu Tiecheng, and Fang Benren, the four provincial chairmen Zhang Zuoxiang, Wan Fulin, Tang Yulin, and Zang Shiyi, consuls from various countries stationed in Shenyang, Zhang's wife Yu Fengzhi, and other senior civil and military officials arrived at the parade ground one after another. When Deputy Commander Zhang arrived in a car, it was past 1:00 PM. Zhang was wearing a regular military uniform. At that time, 19 salute shots were fired, booming through the air. The military band also played the national anthem. After Zhang Xueliang ascended the podium, Commander Wang Yizhe approached the stage to report everything. Zhang then accompanied the National Government representatives and foreign guests on a tour of the parade ground by car. Then the various teams began the marching formation, which was extremely solemn and grand, more spectacular than last year's Double Tenth parade. It only ended after 2:00 PM. That evening, a celebratory dance party was held at the Beiling Villa from 7:00 PM, where the hosts and guests enjoyed themselves and dispersed. (11th)

The Civil Affairs Department yesterday ordered the Jiangyin County Government to investigate thoroughly and handle it according to law. In addition to holding a memorial service, the school has also engaged lawyer Zhang Xun as legal counsel and sent a letter to the Jiangyin County Government requesting that it be transferred to the Zhenjiang Court for trial.

Local Correspondences

Songjiang

The Provincial Party Department Appoints a New Party Committee: Mi Guangguo, the organizing committee member and training director of the local party affairs, was previously transferred back by order of the province. It is now known that his successor, Zhu Tiexian, has been appointed by the Provincial Party Department and designated as the training director.

Cotton Merchants Robbed on Boats: In the southern townships of the county, more cotton is planted than rice. Now is the time when cotton is on the market, and merchants from various places are carrying large sums of money to the countryside to buy cotton, hoping to make a small profit. On the 15th, a shuttle boat to Pinghu and Shanyang was sailing from Pinghu back to Shanyang when five bandits with Mauser pistols suddenly forced it to stop near Jin Siliang Bridge, boarded the boat, and robbed everyone. None of the passengers were spared. Zhou Jiankang from Jinshanwei was robbed of 1,800 silver dollars, and Chen Kaitai and Lu Hongtai's cotton firm also had over 3,000 yuan in Zhuang banknotes, all of which were looted, resulting in a loss of about 5,000 yuan. The bandits then abandoned the boat with their loot and fled.

Plans to Build a Public Speaking Platform: Whenever there are commemorative festivals and national celebrations, all sectors of society express their enthusiasm. Building a platform for performances costs several hundred yuan, all of which is donated by various agencies. Calculating the annual expenditure on building platforms, it amounts to no less than thousands of gold coins, which is uneconomical. Yesterday, this was discussed at a party-government meeting, and it was decided to build a permanent speaking platform in the public stadium, which would be a one-time expense and would avoid danger. The proposal was approved, and the Construction Bureau was instructed to prepare plans and drawings for review and decision.

Suzhou

Large Pond Village Robbery and Murder: In the Guo Xiang district, about five miles outside Fengmen Gate, in Large Pond Village, around 9:00 PM on the night before last (the 16th), twenty to thirty bandits from the lake, traveling in four or five boats, arrived at Large Pond Village via Golden Rooster Lake and Yellow Heaven Pond, landed, and robbed the homes of villagers Pan Baishou, Xu Huisheng, and others. They shot and killed Xu Huisheng on the spot (Xu Huisheng was only nineteen years old and was supposed to be engaged today (the 18th); his being shot by bandits is truly tragic). They also shot and wounded Pan Baishou in the lower abdomen. After robbing the villagers, the bandits fled back towards Yellow Heaven Pond. The wounded Pan Baishou was sent to the Bo Xi Hospital in Heavenly Gift Village overnight for treatment; his life is said to be in danger.

Jintan County Government Accused of Taking Bribes: The Jintan County Government has recently been sued in the High Court by a woman from the county, Han Cui, who stated that her son, Han Yanggeng, was arrested by the county government for a case. Han Cui tried to get her son released by bribing the county government. The county government accepted a large bribe but still sentenced her son to death. She has petitioned the High Court to send someone to investigate thoroughly. After receiving the petition, the High Court issued a response yesterday (the 17th), stating that the case would be investigated and then decided, and ordered Han Cui to submit a formal lawsuit for further handling.

Ministry of Interior Sends Personnel to Survey Xuanmiao Temple's Reflection Wall: The Xuanmiao Temple's Reflection Wall, whether to demolish or preserve it, has been a long-standing dispute that has not been resolved. Yesterday, it was learned that the Executive Yuan has ordered the Ministry of Interior to send personnel to Suzhou for an on-site investigation before making a final decision.

Wuxi

Murder Case on the Border of Wuxi and Cheng: In Dongjiubao Village, Qingyang Township, on the border of Wuxi and Cheng, at the home of farmer Hua Wenlin, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived around 8:00 PM the night before last. Each bandit carried pistols, knives, and clubs. They used stone bars to break open the front door and entered the house to rob. They stole clothing and silver dollars worth about three hundred yuan. The bandits were not satisfied and took the stolen goods to the neighboring house of Hua Guilin, opened the front door, and entered to rob. Guilin and his younger brother, A’liu, lived together and were farmers with a poor family. Guilin had an adopted son, and A’liu had three sons. At that time, the whole family was terrified and tried to hide. Guilin held a gong to raise the alarm. The bandits were furious and fired two shots, hitting Guilin in the right shoulder, shattering his shoulder bone. He fell to the ground unconscious. When A’liu saw his brother shot, he grabbed the bandits, but the bandits immediately fired a shot that went straight through A’liu’s chest. He fell to the ground and died on the spot. Seeing that they had injured people, the bandits searched and robbed for a long time but found nothing. They left in anger. After being injured, Guilin came to Wuxi for treatment yesterday. Fortunately, although the injury is severe, his life is not in danger.

Petition for Thorough Investigation of Refugees Robbing: Chen Zizhen, a resident of Zhongqiao, Third District (Yangming), is a doctor by trade. A few days ago, fifty to sixty refugees suddenly broke into his house and harassed him, stealing forty-six yuan in paper money, silver dollars, and small change, as well as a woman's fur coat. He reported the incident to the Eighth Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau for investigation. However, Sun Aitang, the patrol officer of the sub-bureau, reported to the county bureau that there was no refugee robbery. After learning this, Chen Zizhen stated that the robbery was a fact, witnessed by many, and could not be dismissed as non-existent. Yesterday, he specially petitioned the county bureau to send someone to investigate thoroughly and quickly recover the stolen goods to reassure the people.

Gang Revenge in the Dark: At the home of Hua Gengshou, a resident of Huangnitou in the northern countryside of Xiyi, around 8:00 PM the night before last, the bandit leader Wang Tinghe gathered more than ten followers, each wielding knives and clubs, and swarmed into the village. They opened the front door of Hua's house, tied up Gengshou, and beat him severely with clubs, leaving him covered in injuries. They then dispersed. Afterwards, Hua Gengshou checked his belongings and found nothing missing. Yesterday, he came to the city by boat and went to the hospital for treatment. According to the villagers there, this nighttime beating by the gang was actually revenge due to a grudge.

Resolutions of the District Chief Conference: The Xiyi County Government held its tenth District Chief Conference yesterday, and resolved the following: (1) Method for Rent Reduction this Year: (A) If there are clear regulations in the provincial regulations on rent payment, handle according to local customs; (B) The county government will issue revised rent payment regulations for each district to follow; (C) Following last year's example, the county magistrate will consult with each district to discuss the amount of rent reduction; (2) District clerks arbitrarily increase fees for collecting registers: It was resolved that the county magistrate should order the Finance Bureau to take measures to ban this practice; (3) Corrupt practices such as new township chiefs taking a commission on rice rations: It was resolved that the county magistrate should order the Finance Bureau to strictly prohibit this; (4) The date for township chief appointments should be changed to the Gregorian calendar: It was resolved that the county magistrate should notify the Finance Bureau to comply; (5) This year's autumn harvest is abundant, and each district should implement grain storage to prevent famine.

Wujiang

Formal Appointment of the Fourteenth Squad Leader: Du Jingwu, the leader of the Fourteenth Squad and the First Platoon of the Provincial Water Police stationed in the county, was killed by bandits. The vacancy had not been announced until yesterday, when news from Zhenjiang stated that the Civil Affairs Department had promoted Xu Boying, the leader of the Eleventh Squad, to be the leader of the Fourteenth Squad, and Lu Zhaosheng, the leader of the Fifteenth Squad's First Platoon, to be the leader of the Fourteenth Squad's First Platoon.

Kidnapping of a Doctor in Xietiangang: Cheng Xiqi, a traditional Chinese medicine doctor from Xietiangang, Shengze County, was kidnapped the day before yesterday by bandits posing as patients. They asked Cheng to come to their house to see a patient. Cheng went with his fourteen-year-old son. After they had gone about a mile, a bandit boat suddenly caught up and kidnapped both Cheng and his son. Before leaving, they told Cheng's boatman to quickly inform Cheng's family to prepare 10,000 yuan for ransom.

People in Nanmiao Oppose the Release of Robbery Criminals: On the evening of the tenth of last month, the entire town of Nanmiao in Wujiang was robbed by bandits. The Civil Affairs Department set a deadline of fifteen days to solve the case, but no bandits have been caught to date. On the seventh of this month, a Chen reported that the robbers from the Nanmiao robbery were hiding in Yanmu, near Wuzhen. Sha Zhongnan, the head of the Public Security Sub-Bureau, and Niu Xiqing, the district chief and head of the Anti-Banditry Bureau, went to arrest them and captured four people and found a large amount of stolen goods. However, for some unknown reason, they were immediately released. The merchants and residents of the town were extremely angry when they heard about this and decided to send representatives to question them. They did not receive a satisfactory answer. Therefore, all the merchants and residents of the town were extremely indignant and decided to send representatives to the Civil Affairs Department and the County Government to petition for the removal and investigation of Sha Zhongnan and Niu Xiqing. It is reported that the representatives have already set off.

Nantong

Abolition of the Jiangbei Guerrilla Headquarters: Liu Zuhan, the commander of the Jiangbei Guerrilla Force, resigned from the General Headquarters, and his resignation was approved. The headquarters was abolished immediately.

Guanren District Chief Accused of Extortion: He Wenqiu, the district chief of Guanren, was sued in the County Court by Cheng Tingjian and others for defrauding them of money. After questioning by Prosecutor Zhu, He and his assistants Bao Cigang and Ge Jueren were detained in the detention center.

Kidnapping in Langshan District: At 1:00 AM on the 16th, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived at the Lu Hong Gate in Langshan District in the southern countryside. They destroyed the telephone at the police watch post and stormed into the Yin Shuntai pig business to rob. Before leaving, they kidnapped Wu Huang, the wife of the owner of the Yongtaichang timber business, accountant Lu Hongquan, and pig business accountant Sha Yongsheng, a total of four people. The police squad chased them to the New Harbor Town and captured one bandit named Yang Er, along with a rifle, thirty-eight bullets, and a live pistol. All were sent to the county. The remaining bandits fled by riverboat with the hostages.

Trial Concluded in the Rotten Corpse Case at Tongzhong: A rotten corpse was found in a Taiping tank at the Provincial Nantong Middle School. It was purchased by the school for two yuan from Yan Sheng, a poor household. After an investigation by the county court prosecutor, Yan Sheng was prosecuted for stealing a corpse from an abandoned tomb to get money, which is a crime of violating a corpse. On the 16th, Judge Chai of the Criminal Court held a trial and questioned Gu Zhenxian, the administrator of the school's instrument room, and school servants Chen Da and Li Da, about the incident. After the debate ended, Prosecutor Du stated that Yan Sheng should be punished under Article 262, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. The court announced that the verdict would be delivered on the 22nd.

Jiangyin

Proposals for the Provincial Winter Defense Conference: The Civil Affairs Department will convene a provincial winter defense conference on the 20th of this month. Jiangyin is included in the first group. County Magistrate Li and Public Security Bureau Chief Li will go to the province on the 19th. The County Government has fifteen proposals. The important ones include connecting Jiangyin to the provincial long-distance telephone network and preventing famine victims from Jiangbei from smuggling salt. The Public Security Bureau has seven proposals. The most important proposal is to use the first company of the police force to suppress bandits. During the winter defense period, the countryside will be cleared.

Two Cases Open for Trial, Summons Witnesses: The county government has scheduled the case of Ji Shashi suing Jiang Hong for suspected fraud to be heard on the 18th. Yin Zhongren, Chen Zhongda, Mei Anlan, and Yan Hongzhuang have been summoned for questioning. Yesterday, court police went to summon Mei and Yan, but both were not at home. In the case of Cai Rushan, the county government has scheduled the hearing for the 25th and summoned Zhu Shuping, Chen Danhua, Liu Asi, and Ling Yun to court for questioning.

Zhu Tinghua Becomes Director of the Relief Home: After Jiang Hong, the director of the relief home, resigned, he was taken into custody for investigation in the Ji Hewa bribery case. The position of director was temporarily held by Chen Lan, the deputy director. Because Chen was not capable enough, he firmly resigned to County Magistrate Li. Now, Zhu Tinghua (from Danxiang), a respected elder, has been hired as the director of the relief home. The letter of appointment was personally delivered by County Magistrate Li on the 15th, and Chen was ordered to serve concurrently as the director and prepare to hand over all matters managed by former Director Jiang.

Finance Bureau Investigates and Replies on Establishing a Ship Tax Bureau: The Finance Bureau previously received an order from the Department of Finance to investigate the petition from more than ten people in Cheng, including Shi Yulin, requesting the establishment of a ship tax bureau in Jiangyin and recommending Huang Huafu as the director. It was ordered to investigate and report how much Jiangyin could collect in donations each year and the situation of ships entering and leaving the port. Director Shen then sent staff member Xu Zhaomei to investigate in detail with the Chamber of Commerce Shen Weiru. According to Shi Yulin's report, the annual ship tax revenue would be 10,000 yuan, but there was no certainty. After consulting with the merchants and residents, they all said that the ship tax should be regulated by the provincial department to implement a unified approach throughout the province. If Jiangyin were to implement it first, the method would not be appropriate. The Finance Bureau submitted a reply to the Finance Department for handling.

Small Conflict Between Group Police at Tianxing Bridge: The patrol officers of the Fourth Platoon of the Twenty-Sixth Squad of the Water Police stationed at Tianxing Bridge in Taixing County saw five people in a small hotel at 10:00 PM the night before last. They were wearing military uniforms under their clothes and carrying boxed pistols and symbols. When questioned about their origins, they said they were serving in the Tianxing Bridge Dragon King Temple Security Corps. The patrol officers released them. At 12:00 AM, the water patrol was inspecting passengers on a river steamer when the five people suddenly came to obstruct them and made things difficult for the water patrol. They reported to Platoon Leader Lu Lin, who arrested the five people and took them to the department. Three people escaped and fired their guns as a warning. The two remaining were temporarily detained at the squad headquarters. Unexpectedly, the escaped militiamen invited dozens of people to surround the squad headquarters, entered, and beat them. Platoon Leader Lu Lin was also injured. The patrol officers came to Cheng on the 15th and reported to Shen Hualong of the Twentieth Brigade, who sent personnel to Tianxing Bridge to investigate and handle the matter further.

Fengxian

Fake Committee Member Arrested in Fengxian: Hu Guojun, a fake committee member who had pretended to be from the Ministry of Interior's Institute for the Blind, Deaf, Paralyzed, and Disabled, which was established in Changshu County earlier this month, and defrauded a large sum of money, came to Fengxian from Shanghai the day before yesterday. He first went to the County Government to meet with County Magistrate Shen, asking him to order the various district offices to assist in soliciting donations from wealthy gentry to carry out his fraudulent activities. Today (the 16th), County Magistrate Shen discovered the flaw and ordered the police to arrest him for questioning. He confessed that he had indeed raised funds for orphanages in Changshu more than ten days ago. County Magistrate Shen immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau to detain him temporarily and telegraphed his superiors for instructions on how to handle the matter. He also sent a letter to the Changshu County Government, detailing Hu Guojun's age, appearance, and the official letters and donation booklets he carried, to confirm whether he was the fake committee member that the Ministry of Interior had telegraphed the county to arrest.

Zhenjiang

Jiangsu Province's County Party Affairs Funding Levels: The Jiangsu Province Party Rectification Committee has revised the Party affairs funding for each county and sent it to the Provincial Government. The Provincial Government has ordered the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments to comply. The list of county levels and funding amounts is as follows: (Grade A) 1,600 yuan per month for each county, including Zhenjiang, Nantong, Wuxi, Tongshan, Jiangyin, Rugao, Wuxian, Songjiang, Jiangdu, Wujin, and Yixing (11 counties); (Grade B) 1,200 yuan per month for each county, including Changshu, Suining, Shanghai, Jiangning, Yancheng, Nanhui, Funing, Danyang, Huaiyin, Jiading, and Suqian (11 counties); 1,000 yuan per month for each county, including Fengxian, Taixing, Baoying, Wujiang, Jingjiang, Jintan, Qingpu, Guanyun, Shuyang, Lianshui, Xiaoxian, Qidong, Haimen, Baoshan, Kunshan, Huaian, Fengxian, Gaoyou, Taixian, Dangshan, Xinghua, Siyang, Jurong, Jiangpu, Liyang, Taicang, Ganyu, Jinshan, Pixian, Peixian, and Chongming; (Grade C) 800 yuan per month for each county, including Yizheng and Gaochun (2 counties); 700 yuan per month for each county, including Donghai, Liuhe, Chuansha, Yangzhou, Lishui, and Dongtai (6 counties). The total amount of Party affairs funding for the above 61 counties is 67,600 yuan.

Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department Reassigns County Magistrates: Huang Cishan, the magistrate of Shuyang County, recently sent personnel to the province to request his resignation because the people and land in the county were not suitable for him. Hu, the director of the Civil Affairs Department, considered his resignation to be firm and ordered him to switch positions with Gong Xikui, the magistrate of Suining County. Wang Guanxian, the magistrate of Funing County, was recently sued by the people of the county for a case. Wang felt uneasy in his position and came to the province the day before yesterday to request his resignation. The Civil Affairs Department approved his resignation yesterday and appointed Lu Jixi, who was recorded as a candidate for future appointments, to succeed him. Wang has returned to Fu to handle the handover, and Lu plans to go to the county to take over in the coming days.

Suining County Party Committee Comes to the Province to Beg for Troops: Liu Rongduo and other bandits in Suining County recently broke through Guanlao Temple and Chenxu. The night before last, they occupied the important town of Gaozuoshi in the east of the city. The county police force was weak, and the city defense was extremely critical. The county government convened an emergency meeting of various public law organizations and publicly elected Zhang Minquan, a member of the County Party Committee, to come to the province to beg for assistance. Zhang arrived in the province yesterday and rushed to the Provincial Government's Civil Affairs Department to report the bandit situation and request that a team be sent to rescue them. Since Chairman Ye was in Beijing and had not returned, he did not receive any instructions. He plans to go to the Provincial Government again today to meet with the chairman and request that troops be sent to the county.

Changshu

Principal Offender in Parricide Case Dies in Prison: The case of Cai Yizhi from Baoben Street in this county, which caused a stir in Su and Yu, plotted to kill his stepmother. After the county sentenced Cai and others to imprisonment, they appealed to the High Court, which upheld the original verdict. Cai and others still refused to accept it and appealed to the Supreme Court, which sent it back for retrial. As a result, Cai Yizhi was sentenced to death for the crime of plotting to kill a direct ascendant. The rickshaw puller Qian Zengzeng was also sentenced to death for murder. Cai's wife, Jin, and concubine, Li, were sentenced to life imprisonment for helping to plot the murder. Cai and others still refuse to accept the verdict and have hired a lawyer to appeal to the Supreme Court again. However, this case has been going on for three years. News has been received from Suzhou that Qian Zengzeng, the principal offender in the case, is still being held in the Third Prison. Because he felt there was no hope of survival, he fell ill from worry. His illness suddenly worsened in September, and he began to rave. Doctors treated him in vain, and he died in prison at 7:00 PM on the 12th of this month. Prison Warden Ding Lei reported the matter to the Wuxian District Court for investigation, and the body has been placed in a coffin. However, it is said that this case will be significantly affected after the death of the principal offender.

Yangzhou

Bandits Rob Yongxin Fan Shao Steamer: On the morning of the 14th, the Yongxin Company's Fan Shao class steamer, which operates between Fan and Shao, was robbed by bandits in the Qiushuge area. It is now known that dozens of bandits, dressed in a variety of clothes, carried four Red Cross flags and more than ten rifles and boxed pistols. They ordered the steamer to dock on the shore, and more than twenty of them came aboard, dismantled the engines and threw them into the river, and searched the passengers and crew members of the steamer, none of whom were spared. Some were left with only short shirts and pants. They left at around 4:00 PM.

Reasons for the Replacement of the 133rd Brigade Commander: Rumors of the removal of Liu Hanzhen, the commander of the 133rd Brigade stationed in Yangzhou, have been circulating for some time. It was not until the night before last (the 15th) that it was realized. The new brigade commander, Li Moan, has already arrived in Yangzhou to take up his post. There are various rumors about the reasons for Liu's removal, but according to a recent telegram from the Ministry of Finance to the Lianghuai Salt Transport Office, the change may be related to this. The original telegram stated: "According to reports, the troops stationed there have privately transported 7,000 dan of salt, which is a violation of salt laws. We have telegraphed General Commander Chiang to investigate and handle the matter. The Transport Commissioner should notify the merchants and people to be aware that they must not privately buy or sell salt and be accomplices in prohibited activities, which will result in punishment. If there is any smuggling out of the country, please investigate the route and consult with the anti-smuggling military police to intercept it in separate directions."

Jiaxing

Verdict on Attempted Kidnapping: The Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau cracked a case of attempted kidnapping on Yangguan Street on June 7 of this year, arresting Shi Yiquan, Bian Dingfu, Zhang Gengsheng, and three other suspects. After preparing documents and sending them to the Provincial Government Security Office for investigation, it is now known that the case has been clearly investigated. Shi Yiquan, who attempted to kidnap, should be sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment and deprived of public rights for twelve years in accordance with the Regulations on Punishing Kidnappers and the Criminal Law. Bian Dingfu and Zhang Gengsheng were found to be unrelated to the case and were declared innocent. In addition to being sent to prison and released separately, the original files of the case were sent to the county for verification yesterday.

County Finance Bureau Director to be Transferred to Hangzhou for Questioning: Reliable news has been circulating in political circles that Yan Dawei, the director of the Jiaxing County Government Finance Bureau, will be transferred to the position of director of the Hangzhou County Finance Bureau. After receiving this news, Yan went to the province yesterday to discuss everything.

Gaoyou

Youxing Steamer Almost Robbed Again: The Youxing steamer, founded by the Gaoyou Construction Bureau, has been robbed by bandits three times since it began operating. At 8:00 AM yesterday, it departed from Gaoyou for Xinghua. At around 10:00 AM, when it arrived near Xinzhuang, two farmers on the shore suddenly appeared, looking flustered, and came from the east. Seeing the steamer sailing east, they warned the steamer not to proceed, saying that there were several bandit boats about a mile away, with more than a hundred bandits. The driver thought it was nonsense and continued to sail. At one point, the passengers shouted in alarm and asked to turn back. Unexpectedly, the steamer had been spotted by the bandits. As the steamer turned around, the bandits suddenly fired a shot. Fortunately, the steamer was moving very fast and was not hit. The shell landed in the water about two feet away from the stern, with a loud bang, splashing water everywhere. Seeing that the shell had missed, the bandits abandoned the boat and went ashore, firing their guns and chasing after them. The steamer then opened full throttle and sailed into the harbor, avoiding the disaster. It is now said that the Construction Bureau is considering permanently suspending the service due to the frequent robberies.

Robbery of Rice Boat Kills Entire Family: In the northern countryside of San Duo Town, in this county, two brothers surnamed Wu, the younger brother bought more than ninety shi of rice and grains in San Duo the day before yesterday and transported them to Taizhou for sale. The next day, the older brother also went to Taizhou fully loaded with rice and grains. When he arrived at the Taizhou grain shop, he saw his younger brother's boat parked at the dock, but the rice had not been unloaded. No one was seen on the younger brother's boat, only several tall and strong men, all of whom were unfamiliar. He suddenly became suspicious and secretly questioned the shop owner, who was also surprised to learn of the change and reported it to the Public Security Bureau. The bureau sent police to arrest eight people and sent them to the county government. The older brother also surrendered himself to the authorities. The judge opened the court for trial, and the bandits had no way to deny it because the Wu brother confronted them in court. They then confessed that they had tied up the entire family of five on the boat and thrown them into the river in an area more than twenty li away from San Duo in this county. They then transported the boat's rice and grains to the Rice and Grain Store in Taizhou for sale, and so on. After the interrogation, they were ordered to be chained and imprisoned. Wu immediately returned to his village and sent people to the river to retrieve the five bodies and transport them back for burial.

Education News Highlights

Ministry of Education Petitions for Interpretation of the Civil Service Appointment Regulations

The Ministry of Education submitted a petition to the Executive Yuan regarding whether the fourth paragraph of the fourth article of the Civil Service Appointment Regulations should be interpreted or amended, requesting that it be forwarded to the Legislative Yuan for review. The petition stated that the second paragraph of articles five, six, and seven of the Regulations on the Screening and Review of Incumbent Civil Servants, promulgated by the National Government on October 30, 1929, and the fifth paragraph of article three of the Civil Service Appointment Regulations, promulgated by the National Government on October 29, 1929, stipulated that civil service graduates must come from schools approved by the Ministry of Education. However, the fourth paragraph of the fourth article of the Civil Service Appointment Regulations only stipulates "graduates from domestic or foreign universities or higher vocational schools" and does not add the words "approved by the Ministry of Education" to indicate restrictions. In addition to public and registered private schools, there are many unregistered private schools in the country. Graduates of unregistered private schools should not receive the same treatment as graduates of public and registered private schools. This was clearly stipulated in the regulations for private schools promulgated by the Ministry of Education. As for the level of foreign schools, they are also varied and must be reviewed separately. Only those who are deemed qualified can receive the same treatment as graduates of public and registered private schools. According to the fourth paragraph of the fourth article of the Civil Service Appointment Regulations, all graduates of unapproved and unregistered domestic and foreign schools have the qualifications for appointment, which could lead to many malpractices and be difficult to review. The regulations of the Ministry of Education for reorganizing domestic private schools and reviewing foreign private schools will also lose their effectiveness. Although the rank of appointed officials is lower, the positions they hold are also very important, and their academic qualifications should be subject to the same restrictions as those of recommended officials in order to ensure uniformity and fairness. The Ministry of Education did not presume to propose whether the relevant provisions should be interpreted or amended, as they concern the law. It prepared this document and submitted it for review and requested that it be forwarded to the Legislative Yuan for review and compliance.

Jiangsu Education Funding Must Not Be Diverted from Grain Transport Tax

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has stated that the grain transport tax (忙漕正稅) allocated to them is specifically for educational purposes and cannot be diverted for local education expenses. They have submitted a request to the provincial government to convene a meeting to decide on how to maintain funding until alternative sources can be found. The Department of Education's report states that they received a communication from the Department of Finance regarding the provincial government's instruction to the Department of Education in response to requests from Jiangning, Changshu, and other counties’ Education Bureaus to be exempted from remitting 50% of overdue fines collected within the county. It was ordered that the request be approved and communicated to the relevant authorities for compliance. A previous instruction from the provincial government and a communication from your department to the Department of Education regarding this matter were duly acknowledged. Now, in light of the aforementioned reasons, a copy of the instruction is presented, and a formal request is made for your examination and compliance. We have examined the original report, which mentions that the grain transport tax has been allocated to education funding in recent years, referring to the special education funds from land tax. However, according to the decision of the Central Political Council when the land tax was allocated to local revenue, 1.8 million was annually allocated for educational expenses to compensate for the original tobacco special tax. For the past three years, actual revenue has fallen significantly short, and a request has been submitted to your office for assistance. Furthermore, this special fund is for provincial education expenses and is separate from local education expenses. At a time when provincial education funds are severely strained, there is no additional capacity to compensate for the shortfall in local education revenue in various counties. The comprehensive allocation plan proposed in the original report may be difficult to implement. Regarding the request from the Education Bureaus of various counties to temporarily maintain the previous practice of retaining a percentage of overdue fines collected within the county for local education use, the Department has carefully examined the situation. This request is made out of genuine necessity. For over a decade, 50% of overdue fines collected within the county have been allocated to education and included in the education budget. Suddenly transferring these funds to the province would fundamentally shake the local education budget, inevitably causing some educational programs to be suspended. Moreover, the current fiscal year has already begun, and the Department has approved most of the education budgets for various counties. A sudden change would be extremely difficult. The provincial treasury is depleted, as stated in the original report, and should be considered. However, the matter concerns the rise and fall of local education, which falls under the Department's responsibility, and we cannot stand idly by. Until alternative sources of funding can be found, we respectfully request your office to review and issue instructions on how to maintain funding to prevent disruptions to the education budgets of various counties and avoid the suspension of educational programs. This is for the public good. Respectfully submitted.

After the students of Central University (中大) issued a declaration to improve school administration, all the inside stories of the school have been thoroughly understood by all parties. The school's administrative authorities acknowledge the students' intentions were legitimate. However, they believe that the declaration should not have been released because this gives those opposing the school the chance to take advantage and cause the school to fundamentally waver, thereby losing the original purpose of promoting administrative reform. The school is currently planning on how to remedy the situation. Shao Cong, the head of general affairs, and Dai Chongen, the head of accounting, both sent letters to the president of the school requesting that they be immediately suspended for investigation to clarify the truth.

A Record of the Second Day of the Fudan University 25th Anniversary Celebration

▲Awarding of Honorary Degrees

▲Speeches by Yu Youren and Others

Yesterday (the 17th) was the day of the 25th anniversary celebration of Fudan University in Shanghai. From 8:00 AM, guests from all walks of life arrived in an endless stream, creating an unprecedentedly grand occasion for the university. A brief record of the events is as follows:

▲Student Military Parade At 9:30 AM, the drill instructors led more than 500 members of the student army, armed with rifles and live ammunition, in a parade on the large playground. Their uniforms were neat, their steps were unified, and their military bearing was solemn.

▲Guest Luncheon At noon, the university prepared a special feast at its self-operated consumer cooperative to entertain guests from all walks of life and alumni. Many people dined at the cooperative on that day.

▲Chemistry Demonstration Shortly after the luncheon, a horn sounded, and a thick fog filled the sky, obscuring the entire playground and making it impossible to distinguish directions. This was a smoke screen demonstration conducted by the faculty and students of the chemistry department. The audience was amazed and marveled at the spectacle. After about fifteen minutes, the clouds cleared and the blue sky reappeared.

▲Ceremony The ceremony began at 2:00 PM, led by President Dr. Li Denghui, along with guests, faculty, staff, and graduates, accompanied by military music and firecrackers. The audience was thrilled.

▲Conference Officials The presidium consisted of Ma Xiangbo, Li Denghui, and Jin Tongyin. Wen Chongxin served as the master of ceremonies, and Wang Deliang and Li Jushi served as the recorders. Yu Nanqiu, Zhang Yi, Lin Jiyong, Xu Xinfu, Zou Fang, Chen Xiaowen, and Shen Huanzong served as the receptionists. Xu Ping, Wang Zhenhuan, Wang Hongmo, Ling Zhaoming, and Tao Songqin served as the marshals.

▲Attendees Liu Panzhu represented Jiaotong University, Li Qingya represented Tongji University, Liu Shiben represented Jinan University, Ou Yuanhuai represented Daxia University, Wang Jingqi, former minister to Belgium, Xu Xiangshu represented Aurora University, Xu Zeyi represented the Shanghai Education Bureau, Huang Jiahuai represented the National Anti-Opium Association, Liu Zhanen represented Shanghai University, Song Bingyan represented the Academia Sinica, Wu Jiasan represented the Chinese Red Cross Society, Haimhua, a foreigner, represented the Shanghai YMCA, Pan Geji represented the Anqing Fudan Alumni Association, Zhang Xiyao represented the Suzhou Fudan Alumni Association, Li Yunliang represented the Shanghai Alumni Association, and alumni such as Yu Youren, Shao Lizi, Hu Dunfu, Zhou Yueran, Ye Bingfu, Zhang Xihe, Leng Jun, Lin Yimin, Liu Bainian, Zhang Tinghao, Wang Renlin, Zhang Fengzhou, and Li Bingcheng, numbering over a hundred, as well as reporters from various newspapers, the university's entire faculty and students, and guests from all walks of life, totaling over 5,000 people.

▲Order of the Meeting 1. All stand at attention; 2. Play music; 3. Sing the national anthem and school song; 4. Pay respects to the Party and national flag and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen; 5. Recite Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s will; 6. Silent tribute; 7. Chairman Ma Xiangbo delivers a speech; 8. Confer honorary degrees; 9. Representatives from various bureaus deliver speeches; 10. Guests deliver speeches; 11. Play music; 12. Adjourn the meeting; 13. Take photographs.

▲Chairman's Report President Li briefly stated that the history of the university over the past 25 years has been recorded in various publications. The splendor of today is not due to his efforts alone, but to the collaborative spirit of the board of directors, faculty, and alumni. He hoped that everyone would continue to work hard to make Fudan University as famous as Yale University in the United States. Founder Ma Xiangbo explained in detail the meaning of the name "Fudan University" and elaborated on the meaning of the two characters, "Fu" and "Dan," with both humor and depth. President Li then briefly stated that honorary degrees would be awarded to those who have contributed to the university, the Party, the country, or the society.

▲Awarding of Honorary Degrees Those receiving honorary Doctor of Laws degrees were Qian Xinzhi, Yu Youren, and Shao Lizi. Qian Xinzhi is a director of the university, former Vice Minister of Finance of the National Government, and currently Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance, and president of the four banks: Zhongnan, Continental, Salt Industry, and Jincheng in Shanghai. Yu Youren is an alumnus of the university, currently a member of the Central Executive Committee and President of the Control Yuan, and a director of the university. Shao Lizi is an alumnus of the university, currently a member of the Central Executive Committee and Secretary-General of the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters, and a director of the university. Those receiving honorary Bachelor of Arts degrees were Mao Xibi (a graduate of the university's advanced regular course, currently a teacher at Xujiahui Middle School), Dong Bohao (his background is the same as Mao's), Guo Zhiliang (a graduate of the university's preparatory course, who served in the middle school department for ten years), Ye Zhaoting (who studied at the university and served as the director of general affairs, currently the secretary of the Shanghai Land Bureau), Xi Yushu (who studied at the university and is currently an accountant), Zhu Yingpeng (who studied at the university and is currently a supervisor of the Shanghai Party Headquarters), Tang Boqi (who studied at the university and is currently the Director of the Shanghai Finance Bureau), Su Xinzha, and Ji Yingbo (both of whom have served at the university for 20 years).

▲Summary of Speeches Qian Xinzhi said that he felt ashamed to receive a doctoral degree today while being ill. He said that he had not contributed to the university in recent years and felt deeply sorry. He vowed to work harder in the future. Yu Youren said that Fudan University is the "elder brother" of the Republic of China, and its revolutionary spirit is truly outstanding. He also spoke about his own hardships in studying and encouraged young people to be frugal. Shao Lizi said that he had been busy with national affairs in recent years and had neglected his studies. He felt even more ashamed to receive a doctorate and encouraged young people to study hard. Mao Xibi then gave a speech on behalf of those who received bachelor's degrees. Liu Panzhu, representing national universities, Liu Zhanen, representing private universities, and Li Yunliang, representing the Shanghai Fudan Alumni Association, then gave speeches. The meeting then concluded with music.

An individual from the university's anniversary celebration preparation committee told reporters that due to the hasty preparations, inadequate hospitality, limited space, and time constraints, they were unable to properly entertain all the guests and were very sorry. He also said that Shao Lizi brought a donation of 8,000 yuan yesterday morning and that other alumni who served the Party and the country would continue to donate to the school.

The Re-established School of Law at Jinan University

(1) History Since the reorganization and expansion of National Jinan University in the summer of 1927, there have been regulations regarding the establishment of a School of Social Sciences. In the summer of 1928, the organization was revised and changed to the School of Law, and the Department of Political Science and Law was expanded into the Department of Political Science, Law, and Economics. In 1929, the organization was changed again, and each school implemented the establishment of a dean and adopted a separate school administrative system. The School of Law did not have a dean, the Department of Law was made independent, and the Department of Political Science and Economics was merged into the School of Literature. The School of Law was then abolished. Now, this autumn, a Department of Diplomacy and Consular Affairs has been added. Furthermore, because the Department of Political Science and Economics has been divided into two groups, it is no different from having two departments. The number of students has greatly increased, and the School of Law has become substantial. Therefore, the school affairs conference has decided to re-establish it.

(2) Organization The school is now divided into two departments, two groups, and one specialty. Mr. Wang Renlin, a political scientist, has been hired as the dean. Mr. Wang has studied in Europe and the United States for many years and has served in important social positions, giving him rich experience. The curriculum of each department in the school is very rich, and the newly added courses are particularly unique. In addition to the existing faculty, more than 20 new faculty members have been hired. Sun Hanbing is the head of the Department of Political Science and Economics, Shi Jiong is the head of the Department of Law, and Yang Zhenxian is the head of the Department of Diplomacy and Consular Affairs. All of them are the best of their time.

(3) Current Faculty Sun Hanbing, Zhang Yunfu, Zheng Juemin, Ma Chonggan, Zhu Longhui, Sheng Zhenwei, Zhang Zhirang, Shi Jiong, Yang Zhenxian, Cai Jinghuai, Tao Xisheng, Zhu Tongjiu, Yu Nanqiu, Chen Anren, Yuan Jian, Yuan Yibo, Li Mo, Wang Hanzhang, Wen Chongxin, Huang Zhongjian, Li Bingyu, Li Binghuan, Qiu Hanping, Fu Wenkai, Yu Chengxiu, Wei Weiqing, and Mei Jiejie. In addition, there are several specially appointed lecturers, such as Tan Shaohua, a member of the Treaty Committee of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, who teaches on the Organization of Diplomatic Agencies; Dai Ailu, the chief writer of the Bank Weekly, who teaches on Financial Problems and Public Finance; Qian Chengxu, a director of the Science Society of China, who teaches on Chinese Industrial Plans; as well as Dai Xiuzan and Dong Kang, who teach various law courses.

(4) Plans It is reported that Dean Wang advocates that in the future, in addition to focusing on enriching and strictly enforcing the curriculum, improving and creating in academics, he will also pay attention to the training of student discipline, cultivate a true spirit of self-governance, vigorously promote the organization of academic research, and formulate plans for editing various series of books for the school. In the Department of Law, six or seven kinds of books can be published within the year. The school's faculty and staff hold a dinner party once a month to discuss matters related to the school's development and reform.
