The Remote and Proximate Causes of This Aborted Expedition (II) Yu Hengzhi

In May of this year, news of our European trip spread to Southeast Asia. Given the exceptional performance of Lehua last year, Java wired us an invitation to visit Java again, one month before our scheduled departure for Europe, for a performance. We felt that revisiting Java would provide us with the opportunity for more practice and collaboration, and also generate revenue to bolster our financial resources. After repeated consideration, we believed it would be beneficial and without harm. Thus, Lehua entrusted me to handle the arrangements, while the responsibility of recruiting talent was placed on Mr. Li's shoulders. Because Mr. Li had connections with players from all sides, and he had organized the trip to Australia, he was experienced and indispensable.

My trip south to make arrangements concluded quickly and satisfactorily. At the same time, Mr. Li, despite being ill, traveled east to Japan. He also successfully negotiated with many players during the journey. Only a few duties remained unfinished. In mid-June, Mr. Li came south first, intending to personally consult with those in Hong Kong who had not yet agreed to participate in the overseas tour. The star players in Hong Kong were divided between the South China Athletic Association and the Chinese Athletic Association. Out of friendship and goodwill, we unnecessarily sent a notice about the overseas tour to gauge their players' willingness to participate. The Chinese Athletic Association's attitude was outwardly indifferent, but inwardly a small number were doing their utmost to sabotage, doing their utmost to prevent their players from participating, even using threats to make players withdraw. As a result, Mr. Sun and Mr. Wu, who had initially agreed to participate, declined at the last minute for no good reason. Mr. Chen and Mr. Cao, who were determined to participate, developed disagreements with the saboteurs due to their differing ambitions. As for the South China Athletic Association, their relationship with Lehua had always been beneficial. When I returned north from Java, I had sincere and earnest discussions with their former chairman, Mr. He, and former football director, Mr. Liu. They also expressed extreme support and promised to do their best to help. However, the South China team was also scheduled for a short trip to British Malaya. Therefore, the three South China players who had agreed to participate in the overseas tour would have to join us in Java only after the South China matches were over. Based on our friendly relationship, we trusted that there would be no other changes. Who would have thought that they would use a diversionary tactic, harboring ulterior motives?

On July 5th, we gathered three players from Hong Kong, Mr. Cao, Mr. Chen, and Mr. Liang, forming a team. We set sail south from Hong Kong. We dared not bring too many players, because three players from South China were expected to join us later, and Mr. Chen Zhenhe would arrive in a week. Furthermore, wouldn't it be a perfect plan to invite three or four more skilled Chinese players from British and Dutch Southeast Asia when we set off for Europe?

Man proposes, God disposes. Due to successive injuries and illnesses, a tight schedule, and the blow of South China reneging on their agreement, we suffered four defeats in Southeast Asia. Our performance was far inferior to last year. However, this touched the sympathy of the overseas Chinese community in Southeast Asia and the genuine assistance of various football clubs, solving the problem of finding talent for the upcoming European tour. Patriotic sentiments overseas are often more sincere and fervent than those at home. This is true in politics, and it is also true in sports. We were deeply grateful for this kind of care during our disappointment.

The demon of failure was discovered. The main reason for the demon's discovery was that our self-confidence was too strong. We confidently believed that this purely amateur sport was merely for enhancing diplomatic relations and fostering goodwill, and would always be beneficial. Various procedures were not considered too important. Furthermore, Mr. Harris had previously said that we did not need to worry if the English Football Association approved, because the Hong Kong and Shanghai football associations were under the authority of the English Football Association. The Association's agreement to welcome and host us would ensure smooth progress. Therefore, we neglected the procedures. Never did we expect that neglecting these procedures would become the root cause of our failure.

While we were preparing in Southeast Asia to depart for Europe as scheduled, the English Football Association, considering that our team was composed of players from Hong Kong, Shanghai, Singapore, and Java, and that the Hong Kong, Shanghai, and Singapore football associations were affiliated members, sent three telegrams to these three locations, asking for their opinions. The Shanghai Association telegraphed that they did not object. Singapore also expressed support. However, the Hong Kong Association, due to its own financial concerns and the encouragement of some saboteurs, telegraphed back that they could not agree. As a result, the English side developed great doubts and telegraphed our team, instructing us to postpone our departure by two weeks.

After a team meeting, we felt that there was not enough time to explain. It would be better to telegraph back to England, stating that our team only consisted of players from Shanghai, Singapore, and Java, and that no players from Hong Kong were participating. The Hong Kong Association's consent was therefore irrelevant. We stated that Hong Kong had no players because Mr. Cao was previously a strong player for San Yu, and Mr. Chen had recently assisted Lehua. Both could be considered Shanghai players. As for Mr. Liang, he could also be considered a member of Lehua, because amateur players can play anywhere at any time. He was in Hong Kong last year, but who knows if he will be in Shanghai next year? After sending the telegram, we thought everything was fine. However, the guarantor on the English side became apprehensive about our strength because no one from Hong Kong was participating, and further telegraphed us, asking us to postpone the tour until February of the following spring for further reorganization. Therefore, we, who were ready to depart, had no choice but to return home.

The above is the reality of the situation. I believe that if Hong Kong had not obstructed us, and had not expressed opposition like the Shanghai and Singapore associations, this European and American tour would have achieved satisfactory results. Because the problem of talent was easily solved. We received mutual support from various Chinese associations in Southeast Asia, who allowed us to borrow as many good players as possible who could take leave. The goalkeeper was Yang Ajiu, a representative of Singapore; the defense included Zhang Xulong from Java, Cai Wenli and Xu Ahui, representatives of Singapore; and the forward line included Ye Songling, a representative of Kuala Lumpur, Chen Meian, a player from Malaya; and Feng Wenxun, a representative of Singapore. Adding our original strength, although we cannot guarantee many victories, we could at least give foreigners a good impression. In my opinion, Hong Kong could have only used three or four players at most. Therefore, in terms of strength, this team could be considered to include seven or eight of the national team players. If we reorganize again in the future, I dare not predict whether we can have such strength again.

The news of the team's return home naturally elicited a lot of sympathy and pity. However, there were also many who gloated. Their intentions and motives are truly incomprehensible. Recently, some have even suspected that the players were being paid. The Hong Kong Association has further suspended the playing rights of Mr. Cao, Mr. Chen, and Mr. Liang. On what basis do they allege that the three gentlemen were being paid? I am also baffled. Because the treatment of our members on this trip was based on the old practice of the Australian tour. The Australian tour did not hinder amateur status, and this time was the same. Although Lehua had very satisfactory economic results, this was all the club's public property, which would be used for developing club affairs in the future and had nothing to do with any player. What the players received was nothing more than the necessary travel expenses.

Indeed, there is a lot of right and wrong in our society. Even in the field of sports, we cannot escape this common rule. I believe that in whatever we do, as long as we can be true to our conscience, we can carry on with a fearless spirit. Success or failure, and the praise or criticism of others, do not need to be fussed over. Moreover, we are prepared for infinite sacrifices in doing this kind of work.

Although the expedition has been aborted, there is still a possibility of continuing the voyage. Although we did not achieve our goal this time, we spent a lot of money and energy. We have at least broken down a difficult barrier on the path of future expeditions for those who come after us. I hope that the National Sports Association of China can rekindle the embers of this failure in the future, and instill the spirit of China's new youth into the minds of those foreigners who often call us sick men. In that case, although we failed this time, there will eventually be someone to succeed, and we can find some comfort. Why do I propose that the Sports Association handle it? Because the Sports Association is the highest sports authority in our country. In the future, when negotiating with the English side, we can avoid the kind of obstacles that required the consent of Hong Kong, Singapore, and Shanghai this time. Moreover, I think that using the name of the Sports Association to recruit talent will definitely have satisfactory results. The continued voyage of the expedition is my sincere wish.

The football season at sea has begun again. Some of Lehua's strong players have transferred to Zhenru due to school-related reasons. Lehua has suffered such a blow, and its strength has naturally decreased significantly. Whether Lehua can form a team at all is a question for many who care about it. There are also those who are overly sensitive and say that there are disagreements within Lehua and that cracks have appeared in the football community. This is all a very unconscious kind of argument. I believe that Lehua must continue to participate no matter what. Because although thinning out the original strength now makes it difficult for both sides to achieve excellent results, it has now created eleven more positions to train new talent. The future achievements will definitely be limitless. Therefore, this method of going our separate ways but ultimately converging is the best.

I have always been extremely opposed to bringing up the past. However, this time I will make an exception. I want to use the remaining space here to say a few words that I really don't want to repeat about the rights and wrongs between the South China Athletic Association and us regarding this matter.

Everyone knows that the friendship between South China and Lehua has always been very deep. Every time we pass through Hong Kong, we receive warm hospitality from South China, with the atmosphere of being one family. Who would have thought that this expedition would cause endless rights and wrongs?

When I was making arrangements in Java and returning to Shanghai, I discussed the matter very frankly with the then chairman and football department heads, Mr. He and Mr. Liu, in Hong Kong, treating them as brothers. Mr. He and Mr. Liu were kind enough not to reject us, and fully agreed, expressing their sincerity in cooperating. Even when we departed in early July and passed through Hong Kong, they sincerely expressed their intention to support each other at the South China tea party. Later, when I arrived in Southeast Asia, I personally met with Mr. He and Mr. Yu, the leaders of South China, and asked them when the matches would be over and when the players could join our team. Unexpectedly, at that time, Mr. He and Mr. Yu said that the association had not given instructions and could not comply. Seeing their attitude, I knew that they intended to do so deliberately. More talk would not help. So I had to leave it at that.

Japanese Rice Shipped to Shanghai

▲ The Second Batch Will Be Shipped Soon

▲ News from the Japanese Side. Guowen News Agency reports that after the first batch of 18,300 stones of Japanese rice arrived in Shanghai, the municipal government decided to ban it, and the situation was not good. The second batch of Japanese rice scheduled to be shipped to Shanghai has now changed its course and stopped shipping to Shanghai to prevent detention. According to Japanese sources yesterday, the second batch of Japanese rice to be shipped to China, about 20,000 stones, was loaded onto Mitsubishi company ships in Osaka yesterday and shipped to Hong Kong, where it will be imported and landed because Hong Kong has not yet been banned. However, the number of loads and the name of the ship are very secret, and it will still need to be transshipped to Shanghai in the future.

▲ Mr. Ye Huijun's Opinion. Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau has strictly prohibited the sale of Japanese rice shipped to China. A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency visited Mr. Ye Huijun, a leader in the rice industry, to inquire about his opinion on this matter. According to Mr. Ye, domestic rice production has decreased and prices have fallen this year. But while high grain prices hurt the people, low grain prices hurt the farmers. If large quantities of Japanese rice come to China and drive rice prices lower and lower, agricultural production will inevitably be greatly affected next year, and the result will be no less than that of high grain prices hurting the people. The Japanese rice is coming to China entirely to use China as the final destination for selling old rice. According to the Japanese Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry's October 19th draft plan: (1) The Rice Grain Special Accounting will use 70 million yuan to purchase more than 30,000 stones of new grain; (2) The government's 2.25 million stones of old rice will be sold to China and Europe, etc., even at a slight loss; (3) Farmers will be given loans at relatively low interest rates to avoid having to rush to buy things; (4) The rice produced in Taiwan and Korea will be adjusted to prevent Manchurian rice from entering Korea; (5) The effective period of restricting the import of foreign rice will be extended for another year; (6) The import of Siamese rice and North American rice will be prevented. Also, under the third plan to sell the government's 2.25 million stones of old rice, it has been decided to take out 100,000 stones from the Kobe warehouse as samples and hand them over to Mitsui & Co. to be shipped to Shanghai for sale, and another 215 stones will be shipped one after another. It can be seen that the Japanese government, regarding the rice issue, prohibits the import of foreign rice on the one hand, and ships out large quantities of old rice on the other. In order to protect our domestic farmers, we should strictly prohibit Japanese rice from coming to China.

▲ Talk by a Staff Member of the Social Affairs Bureau. Huadong News Agency reports that various circles have been trying to resist the shipping of Japanese rice to China. A reporter from Huadong News Agency visited the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau yesterday and was received by Mr. Sun from the Fourth Section. When asked about the methods of resisting Japanese rice, Mr. Sun said that the Social Affairs Bureau has decided on two methods. One is active, which is to submit a document to the municipal government and forward it to the Central Executive Yuan, requesting that the customs be ordered to increase the import tax rate on Japanese rice so that the price of Japanese rice is higher than that of Chinese rice. Then, even if our people are not prohibited from buying it, they should be deterred. However, the Central Executive Yuan has not yet approved this matter, so active measures have not been implemented. As for the passive aspect, within the scope of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, such as ordering rice merchants to stop buying and rice mills not to mill it. At the same time, the Social Affairs Bureau has sent many staff members to secretly investigate rice mills and rice merchants in the city to see if there are any private purchases or milling. According to the current investigation, after the order was published, it has disappeared. As for the method of investigating and distinguishing Japanese rice, it is very easy. The Japanese rice shipped to China is mostly stored for too long and has turned yellow. Even after whitening, it is far less resistant than Chinese rice. Moreover, Japan does not have rice mills, and what is shipped is pure brown rice, which must be milled by rice mills before it can be sold. Therefore, the investigation will not be difficult. As for the Japanese authorities' repeated statements that the shipping of Japanese rice to China is due to the Japanese economic panic, in order to protect their farmers, they are exporting to China and asking for understanding. However, at this time of abundant harvests in our country, our country cannot accept its request. If their country sells rice due to economic relations to protect the livelihoods of farmers, our country should also give full protection to our farmers. If foreign rice disrupts rice prices, our country's farmers' livelihoods will also be in panic. Mr. Sun also said that rice prices recently, according to yesterday's highest price, the best white rice has fallen to 15.8 yuan, which is not unaffected by the impact of Japanese rice coming to China. Therefore, the Social Affairs Bureau plans to do its best to maintain it between 15 and 16 yuan and not let it fall. If it falls again, the farmers in the interior will inevitably be greatly affected, and they will not dare to plant rice in the spring plowing next year. Then there will inevitably be a rice shortage next year. The social authorities are responsible for protecting farmers and relieving people's food shortages. Therefore, maintaining rice prices is the best way to protect farmers and relieve people's food shortages.

Xiao Case Negotiations Expand

▲ Xiamen All Circles Reject Java Shipping Vessels

Since the incident of the Deputy Chief Officer of the Java Company's Zhibada ship insulting Ms. Xiao of our country occurred, after our newspaper published the details, it has aroused public outrage in all aspects. Recently, the Java Company has still not made any statement on this case. The Java branch here telegraphed the Batavia head office to inquire about how to deal with the case. According to the telegram from the head office, it was determined that Xiao was mentally unclear, and they continued to shirk responsibility and excuses. It was also said that the ship had sent a letter to Ms. Xiao expressing their apologies, saying that the matter had been resolved. When the Seamen's General Union of this port held a plenary meeting on the 15th, the Xiamen seamen's representatives put forward a motion on the Xiao case, requesting the consent of the meeting. It was resolved: (1) to telegraph the International Labor Organization to request its arbitration; (2) to telegraph the central government, ordering the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a protest with the Dutch envoy; (3) the local branch should warn the Java Company to immediately dismiss and severely punish the Deputy Chief Officer who insulted Ms. Xiao, and compensate for the loss of reputation, and guarantee that the same thing will not happen again in the future. All circles in Xiamen have organized support associations for the Xiao case. Since Java ships have a very large business in Xiamen, the Xiamen Public Association has notified the public to sever business relations with Java ships, including not loading goods and not carrying passengers. At the same time, it also warned the Chinese seamen on Java ships to take the initiative to express themselves in order to promote the resolution of the case. In Xiamen, after the establishment of the Xiao case support association, the ships of the Java Company that arrived in Xiamen were unable to load and unload goods and passengers. Recently, there are as many as eight Java ships in Xiamen that cannot work and operate due to the severing of business relations with the public. They have telegraphed Shanghai for instructions, and the Shanghai office has ordered them to temporarily abandon business in that port and come to Shanghai. All eight ships will be able to arrive in Shanghai within these few days.

The Women's Association also believes that this matter is of great importance to women, so it dispatched members Ms. Chen Zhenquan and Ms. Wu Ruohua as representatives to negotiate with the Overseas Chinese Association, intending to convene representatives of various groups to carry out large-scale support activities in the coming days.

Ministry of Finance Explains the Meaning of Suspending Surtaxes

▲It Restricts Provinces and Cities from Arbitrarily Levying National Taxes

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Cotton Cloth Industry Association yesterday, which stated: "Regarding the previous letter mentioning the continued collection of commodity surtaxes by the Jiangsu Provincial Cotton Products Special Tax Bureau, along with an excerpt of a published Ministry document, requesting an inquiry, after telegraphing the Ministry of Finance for instructions, we received a reply from the Ministry of Finance on the 16th of this month. It stated: 'We have received your telegram. The Ministry previously received instructions from the Executive Yuan to order all provincial governments to refrain from levying commodity surtaxes in the future. Any taxes or levies on goods must be approved by the Ministry before implementation. An order to this effect was issued on August [blank] and forwarded to all provincial finance special commissioners, finance bureaus, and municipal finance bureaus. The meaning of this circular is to restrict provincial or municipal governments from arbitrarily levying taxes and levies on goods within the scope of national taxes. Regarding the Jiangsu Provincial Cotton Products Special Tax Bureau’s continued collection of surtaxes as mentioned in your telegram, the Ministry has not received a report detailing the specific circumstances, and has no basis for action. We should await the Jiangsu finance special commissioner’s report after investigation before further action can be taken. You are hereby notified accordingly.' We are enclosing the telegram for your information."

Lecture Notes of Mr. and Mrs. Vandervelde

▲Mr. Vandervelde Lectured at Labor University Yesterday

Mr. Vandervelde, leader of the Second International and Prime Minister of Belgium, visited the National Labor University in Jiangwan yesterday, and at the invitation of the university, delivered a speech in the university's auditorium. The secretary-director of the university, Mr. Peng Xiang, introduced him in Chinese and French, and Mr. Yang Gongda provided interpretation. The lecture lasted for an hour. The main points are recorded as follows: "I am very happy to be able to meet you all today. The secretary-director mentioned that the Chinese Labor University is modeled after the principles of the Belgian Labor University, and that it is the second such university in the world after the Belgian one. This is very accurate. The Belgian Labor University was founded by our Socialist Party. It has two goals: one is to train technical personnel, and the other is to train personnel for social enterprises. These two goals are gradually being achieved. Although the Chinese Labor University is different due to China's circumstances, Mr. Sun Yat-sen once said that China only has the distinction between the very poor and the slightly poor, without capitalists, classes, or workers. However, in reality, there are already capitalists, classes, and workers in China's major cities. These workers lack legal protection and live like cattle and horses. However, I believe that one day they will become aware and organize themselves. Therefore, I hope that in China, under these circumstances, the Labor University, in addition to training specialized technical personnel, should also train technical personnel for social enterprises to realize the demands of the Chinese nation. Although some people in Europe are jealous of you, we in the Socialist Party are looking forward to

your success," and so on.

▲Mrs. Vandervelde Lectured at the Benevolent and Orphanage Society Yesterday

The Child Welfare Advancement Association of China, Department of Child Research, invited Mrs. Vandervelde, former Foreign Minister of Belgium, current leader of the Socialist Party, and chair of the Second International, to give a lecture at the Industry and Commerce Visiting Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce on Hankou Road at 4 PM yesterday. Forty to fifty Chinese and foreign guests attended. Mr. and Mrs. Fu Anlan, principals of the blind children's school, and Chen Zhengfan and Wu Zhou Shujing, executives of the Benevolent and Orphanage Society, served as hosts. Song Wusheng served as the translator. Dr. Luo Yunyan gave a welcoming speech. Mrs. Vandervelde began her lecture, the topic of which was "Hygiene is the Key to Child Welfare." The gist was: "When I was young, I was very concerned about children's health and protection. Later, I studied medicine and became more aware of social medicine. I should first focus on pediatric medicine and devote myself to researching children's health facilities. I am very interested. This time I came to China to investigate the mortality rate of Chinese children, which reaches 15%. And the incidence of congenital diseases and death from tuberculosis and malnutrition reaches 50%, especially among the working class. The reason is that mothers still work in factories during pregnancy, lacking proper care and hygiene. Also, children are made to work in factories before they reach adulthood. It is not like this in European and American countries. Female workers in factories are given assistance in life during pregnancy, and many public hospitals are set up, as well as infant clinics, to examine newborns for congenital diseases and protect them with care. Factories with more than fifty female workers have public nurseries for breastfeeding and absolutely prohibit child labor. During school enrollment, school hygiene includes health checkups for children, and they are often guided to go on outings and absorb fresh air, so that children can receive full education, reduce mortality, and develop healthy citizens in the future."

Silk Factories Agree on Relief Loan Measures

The silk factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai, seeing the foreign silk market in a state of collapse and facing huge losses, have declared business closures one after another. They have publicly discussed and appealed to the government to issue silk industry bonds worth 10 million yuan to provide relief. Representatives have been sent to Shanghai to form a special committee for applying for silk industry relief to handle the application and apportionment matters. Two representative conferences have already been convened, and the general outline has been decided as follows: (1) Relief for the entire silk industry in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai; (1) Request the government to issue bonds, (Name) Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai Silk Industry Bonds, (Amount) 10 million yuan in national currency; (1) Repayment issue, following the customs revenue treasury bond method, with principal and interest to be paid off in five or six years. From the date of issuance, all exported silk will be subject to a surtax of 20 taels of silver per bale to serve as a fund for repaying the bonds. During the repayment period, anyone who is a part of the entire silk industry in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai, regardless of whether it is a newly established factory or an existing factory, should be jointly responsible for the future of the entire silk industry; (1) The distribution of bonds will be based on the number of machines in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai, and will be distributed equally; (1) The distribution procedures and security measures stipulate that those who are eligible for relief are as follows: (1) Those who started operating with new cocoons this year, from June 1st in the lunar calendar; (2) Those who can continue to operate. Those who are not suitable for relief are as follows: (1) Those who have already closed down; (2) Those who do not continue to operate; (3) Those who have not started operating since the new cocoons were listed. Procedures for claiming bonds: (1) Must be jointly signed by the legal representative and the directly responsible shareholders, and bear the obligation to repay. The names and qualifications of the representatives and shareholders must be reported in writing in advance, and valid documents such as partnership agreements or contracts and factory rental contracts must be submitted for review; (1) When claiming bonds, in addition to the signatures of the directly responsible representatives and shareholders, a guarantee letter must be provided; (1) The guarantor's guarantee letter shall guarantee the amount of the loan and the repayment until it is cleared. The above outline has been submitted to Shen Huachen, chairman of the Special Committee for Relief of the Silk Industry, and notified to all silk factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai for their information.

▲Siam Chinese General Chamber of Commerce

▲Annex to Build a National Products Exhibition Hall

We hereby inform your association, and request that you handle it accordingly, and encourage all national product factories to transport products to Siam for display in order to promote them.' We hereby forward this to your association, and request that you handle it accordingly, and encourage all national product factories to transport products to Siam for display in order to promote them."

Renaming of Deeds for the Yingshi Memorial Hall

▲The Lake Society Committee Requests to Change the Account Name

The Shousheng Nunnery on Beijing Road in this city, after the order of the National Government to rebuild the Yingshi Memorial Hall, the Lake Society Committee has been actively carrying out this matter. Recently, Chen Qicai, chairman of the Lake Society Committee, stated that the original deeds of the Shousheng Nunnery base were in the name of Shousheng Nunnery and the former custodian Yang Xinzhi. The original document stated, "We respectfully submit this brief report, the Shanghai Society location and the base of the Martyr Chen Gong Yingshi Memorial Hall, built in the Society location, located on Guizhou Road, Beijing Road, Public Concession, the original Deed No. 83 and Deed No. 84, registered by the British company Tonghe Yanghang, issued two Rights Certificate. Because it is the property of the Huzhou Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai, fellow villager Yang Xinzhi was appointed as the representative to manage it. The house was used by Shousheng Nunnery, which was managed by our society, so the name on the Rights Certificate was Yang Xinzhi Shousheng Nunnery. Now that we are ordered to change its use, the name on this Rights Certificate should be changed. Yang Xinzhi has already passed away. We propose that your government instruct the Ministry of Judicial Administration to instruct the Shanghai Special Zone Local Court to inform Yang Taiyuan, the son of the deceased Yang Xinzhi, also known as Yang Kuihou, and the Lake Society Committee, to change the original note on the Rights Certificate of No. 83 and No. 84 to the name of the Chen Yingshi Memorial Hall of the Lake Society, in order to uphold public property and comply with the final decision."

Reduced Freight Rates for Jianghai Ships

▲Disruptions in the Freight Rates of Cotton Yarn on the Upper Yangtze River This year, the number of foreign merchants' ships on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River has greatly increased. On the Shanghai-Yichang route, Taikoo has five ships, Jardine Matheson has three ships, Nissin has three ships, and Jiejian has four ships. They are competing for the transportation of cotton yarn. Shanghai's transportation of cotton yarn to Yichang is regarded as the best freight rate in the shipping industry. In recent years, due to excessive competition, the freight rate for yarn has fallen sharply. From Shanghai to Hankou, it has fallen to 2 taels 8 qian 8 fen per piece. From Hankou to Yichang, it has fallen to 4 taels 9 qian 5 fen per piece. Last month, Taikoo Company first reduced the freight rate by 4 taels in order to compete for the transportation of cotton yarn transferred from Hankou to Yichang. The Sanbei Company, due to its contracting nature, reduced the freight rate by 3 taels through the manager of the upper Yangtze River. At that time, Nissin Company also joined the competition, actually collecting 6.95% of the freight rate for yarn. As a result, the price of yarn on the upper Yangtze River suddenly became chaotic. Recently, the British Taikoo Company has taken it a step further and made a second major price cut, reducing the freight rate for cotton yarn from Hankou to Yichang from 4 taels to 2 taels. Combining this with the 2 taels 8 qian 8 fen from Shanghai to Hankou, the freight rate for yarn going to Yichang and transshipped in Hankou is only 4 taels 8 qian 8 fen. The price of direct shipping from Shanghai to Yichang is 6 taels 1 qian 3 fen, causing the recent Shanghai cotton yarn transport to Yichang to be repackaged for transshipment in Hankou, which can save 1 tael 2 qian 5 fen per piece. As a result, there is no yarn to transport on direct ships to Yichang. Recently, various customers have questioned the shipping companies about this contradiction. It was heard yesterday that the companies are meeting to discuss remedial measures.

▲Falling Short of Freight Rates for Goods Transported in the North Sea Recently, due to the restoration of the transportation of goods in Tianjin and the cancellation of the double tax, five shipping companies, including Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Nissin, and China Merchants, have each sent representatives to a meeting to discuss and reduce the freight rates for various export goods. The results of the discussion have been determined, and the new freight rates have been drafted and announced: (1) Ironware, 5 qian 1 fen per dan; (2) White sugar, 5 qian 1 fen per bag; (3) Raw cotton, a reduction of 1 tael 6 qian 7 fen; (4) Cotton yarn, reduced to 8 taels 4 qian 6 fen; (5) Waste paper, reduced to 1 tael 2 fen; (6) Cotton seeds, reduced to 1 tael 3 qian 5 fen; (7) Yarn waste, reduced to 1 tael 8 qian 2 fen; (8) Machine cotton, reduced to 6 taels 6 qian 8 fen; (9) Baled machine cotton, reduced to 8 taels 4 qian 1 fen. The customers have been notified and the new prices are being implemented.

Unemployed Stewards of Shifts on Various Ships

▲China Merchants Bureau Formulates Adjustment Measures

The unemployed stewards of the various ships of the China Merchants Bureau requested relief from the Seamen's Union and asked the union to send a letter to the bureau to find a way to resettle them. After receiving the letter from the Seamen's Union, the China Merchants Bureau formulated six remedial measures and replied to the union yesterday. The Seamen's Union still needs to submit these measures to the Reorganization Committee and the Middle Cabin Office for discussion at a meeting before responding to the China Merchants Bureau for a decision. The temporary measures for adjusting the stewards who should be assigned are listed as follows: (1) Stewards who have been assigned to ships for more than half a year and cannot serve on the ship will be subject to these measures. (2) If there is a shortage of stewards on the bureau's sailing ships, or if they have been on leave for more than two months and have not yet returned to work, and stewards who have been assigned to ships for more than half a year and have not served on the ships, the business director of each ship shall report them to the business department. (3) The business department, based on the reports of the business directors, will list the stewards who have been assigned to ships for a long time by sea and river ships and instruct the business directors to resettle them properly. (4) Stewards who have been resettled must be transferred back to serve when the original ship returns. They must not make excessive demands. (5) If the stewards on each ship cannot understand the resettlement issue, causing disputes, the Seamen's Union should be fully responsible for mediation. (6) These measures may be abolished by the bureau at any time when the assignment is over or for special reasons.

Shanghai Political Workers and Students Telegraph the National Government to Punish Duan Heng Severely

▲To Vindicate Luo Cheng, the Former Magistrate of Leiyang County

Yesterday, all the students of the Political Workers Training Institute in Shanghai telegraphed the Central Government, saying, "To the Nanjing National Government, we report that Luo Cheng, a student of the Political Workers Training Institute, was innocently shot and killed by Duan Heng, commander of the Southern Hunan Garrison, while serving as the magistrate of Leiyang County, Hunan. The case has been reported to your government by He, chairman of Hunan, for record. On September 28, Duan Heng, commander of the Southern Hunan Garrison and commander of the 55th Brigade of the 19th Division, suddenly drove by car from Hengzhou to the Leiyang County Government. After meeting with Magistrate Luo, he immediately asked why the people of Leiyang were panicking and fleeing to Hengzhou. He immediately replied that there were communist bandits in the county spreading rumors and disrupting the people's minds. They are currently investigating and arresting them strictly. Before he could finish speaking, Duan took out a gun and shot and killed Magistrate Luo. Duan later submitted a report to the provincial government and a telegram to the Fourth Route Army Headquarters, falsely claiming that Magistrate Luo had abandoned his post and disrupted the rear, and executed him. Although Chairman He knew the truth of the case, he leniently dismissed him in order to maintain the local security of more than 20 counties in southern Hunan, which depended on Duan's department. He was still allowed to temporarily hold his concurrent positions in the hope of redeeming himself through meritorious service. Comrade Luo, as a local official, even if he was negligent, his competent authorities would deal with him. There was no need for the military to overstep its authority. Moreover, Comrade Luo supervised the team's clearance and suppression of bandits day and night during his tenure as county magistrate. He never left Leiyang and never abandoned his post or disrupted the rear. It is absolutely unforgivable to shoot and kill a local official without authorization. If the punishment is still lenient due to local security concerns, then soldiers can kill people with impunity. What is the difference between the national discipline and tatters? We hereby telegraph to your seat, based on the original intention of protecting human rights and the righteous act of upholding the national law, immediately telegraph He, chairman of Hunan, to revoke the previous punishment and sentence Duan Heng to the crime he deserves for murder, in order to warn against violence and promote discipline. The political workers training center students respectfully implore."

University Student Dies Tragically Hit by Songhu Train

▲Liu Zhen'ou, Student of Chih Chih University

▲Crossing the Railway for Lunch at Home

▲Hit by the Train While Trying to Avoid It and Died

Liu Zhen'ou, a student at Chih Chih University on Jiangwan Road, was returning home from school at around 11:55 AM yesterday after class. While crossing the railway in front of the school gate, a train from Songjiang to Shanghai sped by. Liu was unable to avoid it and was thrown more than ten feet by the front of the train, suffering fatal injuries upon impact. The Fifth District Public Security Bureau's Baziqiao Police Station reported the incident to headquarters and requested the court to conduct an autopsy. The deceased was from Shantou, Guangdong, and was a third-year law student at Chih Chih University. As a commuter student, he usually returned to his home at No. 33, Huayuan Street, for lunch every day. Yesterday, he went home as usual, but unexpectedly met with this sudden death. The teachers and students of the university were all saddened by the news. When Liu died, he was wearing a dark blue serge Western suit, black leather shoes, and his head was severely injured, with blood and flesh blurred, a tragic sight to behold.

A Page of Scandalous History of the Son of a Leather Shop Owner

▲The Old Father Thought His Son Was Reliable

▲Unexpectedly, the Young Man Made Bad Friends

▲Entangled with a Female Hostess

▲Squandering Over One Thousand Gold Coins of the Shop's Funds

▲Leaving the Shop Affairs to His Son - Xu Yuhe, a local, owner of Xu Shunxing Leather Shop at No. 229, Disiwei Road, Hongkou, recently fell ill and could not attend to business at the shop. He instructed his eldest son, named Zide, to quit school and help with the shop affairs. Zide was only sixteen years old, quite diligent, and very capable in handling matters. Xu was pleased and rested at home to recover.

▲Falling in Love with a Female Hostess - Unexpectedly, Zide was young and impulsive, and was seduced by his peer friend Zhu Shunjin from Anhui, frequently going to the Tianyun Building of Wing On Company for entertainment. He then fell in love with Zhang Naizhen, a local female hostess in the Peking Opera department, aged twenty. From then on, they spent much time together, and their feelings grew deeper. They often rode motorcycles together for excursions in the suburbs.

▲Renting a Room in a Hotel for Secret Rendezvous - Because they could not fully express themselves in public places, they rented a room in the New World Hotel as a rendezvous point. During their leisure time, they also invited Zhang's colleague, hostess No. 3, Afang, to play mahjong together. As a result, the love between Zide and Zhang reached a boiling point, and they engaged in physical relations. They showered each other with affection, and Zide often bought gifts for Zhang to win her favor. However, Zide's financial resources were limited, so he secretly took and used his father's shop funds.

▲Taking Ambiguous Gender Photos - He also went to a photo studio near the City God Temple with Zhu Shunjin and Afang to take photos. Xu and Zhu dressed as women, while Afang dressed as a man, wearing a Western suit and sitting side by side with Xu. Zhu stood behind them, dressed authentically. At first glance, it was difficult to distinguish their genders. After a few days, Xu, Afang, and female hostess No. 6, Aifeng, took another photo of a scene from the Peking Opera "Yellow Crane Tower."

▲Suspecting His Son Was Kidnapped - This went on for several months, and Xu was constantly involved in the world of female entertainers, but his father knew nothing about it. On the 13th of this month, Zide went to Suzhou for sightseeing and did not come to the shop for several days. When someone reported this to his father, Xu Yuhe suspected that his son had been kidnapped by bandits. He went to Zhu Shunjin to inquire, but Zhu said he only knew that Xu Zide had gone to Suzhou for sightseeing and did not know anything else.

▲Finding Out the Truth After Checking the Accounts - Yuhe went to the shop to check the accounts and discovered that Zide had privately used shop funds amounting to a huge sum of 1,968 yuan. He also found two photos, and finally realized that Zide had been engaging in inappropriate behavior outside. Because Zide and Zhu Shunjin were very close friends and often went out together, he notified the owner of Jin Youji Leather Shop at No. 31, East-West Huade Road, to detain Zhu Shunjin.

▲The Three Were Arrested One After Another - He also reported to the Hongkou Police Station, which sent Detective Chen Baozhong. At 8 PM the day before yesterday, Chen learned that Xu Zide had returned to Shanghai and was still playing in the Peking Opera department of the Tianyun Building. He arrested Xu and Zhang Naizhen and went to Jin Youji to bring Zhu Shunjin to the police station. The police chief ordered them to be detained separately.

▲The Police Station Filed a Lawsuit - Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the Special District Local Court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the police station, explained the case and accused Xu Zide of embezzlement under Article 357, Section 1 of the Criminal Code, and Zhu Shunjin and Zhang Naizhen of defrauding property under Article 363 of the Criminal Code. He then submitted the photos and other evidence. Detective Chen Baozhong then reported the circumstances of the arrest of the defendants, and the plaintiff, Xu Yuhe, testified about the above events.

▲The Deceptive Tactics of the "Ambiguous Gender Gang" - Xu then engaged a lawyer to appear in court, claiming that the plaintiff's son, Zide, was actually under the age of sixteen, ignorant, and easily deceived by others. Zhu Shunjin and Zhang Naizhen are known as the "Ambiguous Gender Gang" in Shanghai. They had already been in cahoots and deliberately lured Zide into their trap to defraud him of money for their own use. He requested that Zide be allowed to be released on bail while awaiting trial.

▲Always Losing in Gambling - When questioned, Xu Zide confessed that he went to the Wing On Company amusement park to relax on the fifth day of the sixth lunar month, where he met Zhu Shunjin. Zhu then introduced him to female hostess Zhang Naizhen to serve tea, and they fell in love. Later, he and Zhang took a car for a ride and rented Room 214 in the New World Hotel, where they played mahjong with Zhu and Afang several times. However, he always lost when gambling.

▲Visiting Friends in Suzhou - Later, he stayed with Zhang at the hotel for several nights. The money used from the shop, about more than one thousand yuan, was all taken by Zhang, who claimed it was for shopping and miscellaneous expenses. He bought a gold watch worth 28 yuan as a gift for Zhang. Zhu did not borrow money from him. He had no improper relationship with the female hostess Afang. The reason for not returning home for the past few nights was that he went to Suzhou to visit friends. After returning to Shanghai, he stayed at the Far East Hotel for two nights, and Zhang came to stay with him one night. The photos were taken with Afang and others at the City God Temple.

▲Denying Staying at the Hotel - Zhu Shunjin confessed that he did not introduce Xu Zide to Zhang Naizhen. The rest of his confession was evasive. Zhang Naizhen confessed that she did not admit to staying with Xu Zide at the World or Far East Hotel. She only played mahjong once. However, Xu was very close to her younger sister, Afang, and she had broken up with him a long time ago.

▲Summoning Witnesses for Further Inquiry - Judge Feng Shide reviewed the confessions and ordered Xu Zide to provide a shop guarantor to be available for questioning at any time. Zhang Naizhen was to provide a 1,000 yuan shop guarantor. Zhu Shunjin was to be held for seven days for investigation, and witnesses were to be summoned for further inquiry.

The Municipal Government to Build the Second Public Housing

▲Planning to Build 400 Units

▲Expected to be Completed by Next March

To ensure the safety of residents and improve the lives of the poor, the Municipal Government proposed the construction of public housing in May of the 17th year (1928). In October of the same year, a committee was established to plan and implement the project. In May of the 18th year (1929), the first public housing with 100 units was completed on Quanji'an Road. For more than a year, the residents who have moved in have not only benefited physically and mentally, but also received guidance from the managers in their daily lives, which has greatly improved their lives. People from China and abroad have praised the project. However, due to the limited location, the relief is still not widespread enough. It is now learned that the Municipal Government has selected a site in the Lujiawan Xietu Road Luban Road area to build the second public housing. In addition to building a large auditorium, office building, and cooperative store, it is planning to build 400 units. Construction began yesterday and is expected to be completed by March next year. It is expected that another 400 poor families will be able to enjoy the joy of living in peace at that time.

The Age Issue in the Freedom of Marriage for Men and Women

▲Lan Xufang is Less Than Half a Year Short

▲Regretting Her Impatience in Prison

Lan Lianchen's daughter, Lan Xufang, a clerk at Helan Foreign Firm, freely married Chen Mingqi. Lan found out and reported it to the police, who arrested them and transferred them to the Local Court. This matter was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that after the preliminary trial by the prosecutor of the Local Court, Chen and Xufang were both detained. The reason for their detention is that Lan Xufang is only twenty years old this year. According to the criminal law, the freedom of marriage without criminal offenses requires that one be twenty years old. That is, one must be twenty-one years old after their birthday to be considered twenty years old. Currently, Lan Xufang is of course less than twenty years old. Therefore, Chen Mingqi is guilty of seducing a woman under the age of twenty for adultery. However, Lan Xufang could have been acquitted, but because she did not want to return to her father, she was detained. Chen Mingqi and Lan Xufang were not unaware of this law. They only knew that they could have freedom of marriage at the age of twenty, but did not fully understand the interpretation of the legal provisions. That is why when Xufang was nineteen years old last year, she was willing to stay in the Women's Association for a year. Only because Xufang's birthday is in February, if she could have waited until February of next year, she would have been fine after only missing half a year. Now, after both men and women have been convicted of a crime, their marriage is even more restricted and cannot be consummated. Therefore, the lawyers of Chen Mingqi and Lan Xufang went to visit them at the detention center yesterday after hearing the news. Lan Xufang still claimed that she had the right to autonomy. After the lawyers explained the law, she regretted her impatience. However, her personal will remains true to her original intention.

Japanese Residents' Anti-Gambling Movement

The day before yesterday afternoon, Japanese community leaders in Shanghai gathered at the Japanese Club to discuss the anti-gambling movement. The Japanese Deputy Ambassador Shigemitsu, Acting Consul General Wangpu, Police Chief Huali, and community business leaders Miyari, Fukushima, Miyazaki, and Lin, and more than forty people attended the meeting to discuss ways to prevent Japanese residents from going to horse racing, dog racing, and other gambling venues. Finally, it was decided that Fukushima, Lin, Miyari, Anju and others would form a committee to formulate a concrete plan, and then work with the Japanese consul to implement it. It is said that the reason why the Japanese community launched the anti-gambling movement was because they saw that countless Japanese residents often went to horse racing, dog racing, and other gambling venues, resulting in various criminal acts such as embezzlement, fraud, and theft. Young store clerks were the most affected. If measures are not taken to stop it quickly, the entire Japanese community will be affected.

Prohibition of Overloading Passengers on Inland River Vessels

The Shanghai County Government recently received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction, stating, "In order to comply with the order, it has recently been found that inland river vessels often seek short-term profits and overload passengers, resulting in dangerous situations. A strict prohibition order should be issued to ensure safety. In addition to sending it out separately, it is hereby issued a proclamation ordering the county magistrate to instruct all shipping companies to affix the number of passengers stipulated by the Customs on the ship in a place where passengers can easily see it. The number of passengers must comply with the number limit on the sign, and the proclamation should be forwarded to the shipping companies, ordering them to install glass frames and hang them in the ship's cabins for compliance and easy inspection. The county construction bureau chief should also be supervised to strictly implement it, and a report should be submitted for investigation. This is the order."

Falling Rice Prices in Shanghai

▲The Source is Becoming More and More Abundant

The price of rice in Shanghai has gradually decreased recently. New rice from various production areas has been harvested, and the harvest is unusually abundant, so it has been transported to Shanghai for sale, resulting in crowded arrivals. The arrival of new and sharp rice is even more prosperous. Su, Song, Jia, and Hu have 20 arrivals every day, and dozens of trains of Huaiyang guest rice are loaded every day. Therefore, the goods on the market are accumulating more and more, but sales are weak. The stores see the number of arrivals flourishing and the market price falling, so they are watching the purchase to avoid losses. Therefore, there is a market but no transactions. The owners see the market sluggish and need to sell quickly, so they have to reduce prices, which makes the market even more tired. The largest sales of Su Tong new rice are 14.56 yuan, and Songjiang new rice is 13.23 yuan to 13.56 yuan. The new rice has the largest number of arrivals and inventory, and it has reached 10 yuan for entry and 9.56 yuan to 9.78 yuan. However, Huaiyang telegrams are urging distributors to sell the goods quickly, several times a day. According to the industry, the source is so prosperous at the beginning of the new rice season. If there is no packing and hoarding on the stack in winter, the price of japonica rice is expected to fall to around 10 yuan.

After Director Shen interrogated them, the case was transferred to the Local Court for trial yesterday.

Notice on the Improvement of Car Services on Two Railways

In order to sort out and improve the car service methods, the car service offices of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways specially issued a notice to the station staff yesterday, "(1) The mobile telephone on the Beijing-Shanghai line is specially installed with test wires at Shanghai North Station and Nanjing Station. Regarding the mobile telephone on the car, it should be tested before the car starts. The case has been notified to the public on the first day of last month. Now, for the convenience of testing, this test wire is specially placed at Shanghai North Station and Nanjing Station. Shanghai North Station is installed at the end of the platform near the station car yard, on the second to third poles, and Nanjing is installed on the tenth to eleventh poles at 310 kilometers. All car guards should be aware of this. (2) Method for loading materials. Regarding the engineering materials car, it has been ordered to comply with the special train schedule No. 355 on July 28 of this year. Now, in order to facilitate the track supervisor to arrange the loading of cars at the station in advance, the stationmaster of the departure station should also notify the relevant engineering office personnel by telephone or other written methods one night before the empty car arrives at the arrival station. After the empty car arrives at the arrival station, it must be handed over to the engineering office personnel for loading the next morning to avoid delay.

Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Locomotive Derailment

▲The Railway is Slightly Damaged

▲Repaired by Rescue Vehicle

At 8:50 PM the night before last, the 27th night freight train from Zha Kou to Shanghai on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway arrived at Maigen Road. At about 9:00 AM the next morning, the freight train drove into the track next to the freight station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou line to unload the goods, and then the locomotive was disconnected and driven alone to the locomotive room. While passing through the branch road of the freight road, it suddenly derailed, damaging the road. Therefore, traffic between Maigen Road and Fanwangdu was blocked. The station master urgently telegraphed the North Station car service and locomotive chiefs, who rushed to send a rescue vehicle to the accident site to repair it. At 11:10 AM, the rescue vehicle from the North Station arrived at Maigen Road, first repaired the track, and then used a crane to lift the derailed locomotive into the track. The repairs were completed and traffic was restored at 1:25 PM.

Sock Factory Partner Leaves a Letter and Flees

▲Said He Was Going to Commit Suicide

Fang Shouchun, a partner at the Gongping Sock Factory at No. 171 Guangdong Road, was suddenly hit by a blow recently. He suddenly fled at 1:00 PM the day before yesterday. After opening it, he found that it was a letter left by his younger brother, saying that he was going to commit suicide and would say goodbye to everyone. After reading it, Jiepu was shocked and feared that he had committed suicide by jumping into the river. Preliminary Hearing of the Casia Case

The Great American Evening Post said that in the case of the American Casia being killed at the intersection of Bazilukou, the murderer, Filipino Tupias, was again held for a preliminary hearing in the US Consular Court this morning (17th). The witness Ampu initially stated that Casia punched the defendant in the face twice after getting off the rickshaw, which led to the quarrel. In response to the prosecutor's inquiry, he also stated that the defendant first shouted at Casia to get off the rickshaw. According to Frank, who was traveling with Casia that day, there were two other Filipinos punching him at the time, so he was not very clear about the defendant's actions. It was not until the perpetrators dispersed that he saw Casia walking towards the center of the street. He also said that Casia's car was about 20 feet behind his car, and he only heard Casia telling his car to slow down and wait for a minute, but he did not mention that the defendant had told the deceased to get out of the car. The hearing continued in the afternoon, and many witnesses were called.

Sangmei's Song and Dance Collection

▲Perfectly Displayed

Yesterday at 5:30 PM, Sangmei Dance School performed the second day of the "1930 Love Song and Dance Collection" at the Summer Peke Theater on Jing'an Temple Road. Thousands of Chinese and Western gentlemen and ladies flocked to watch, and the hairpins and clothes were fragrant, which was a grand occasion. The entire audience was focused on this crystallization of beautiful art of song and dance, watching without blinking. The entire performance was divided into two parts, each part divided into eleven programs. The scenery and costumes were rich and magnificent, all reaching the best. There were more than 50 dancers, with faces more beautiful than flowers and voices as delicate as orioles. When they danced gracefully, they were like startled geese, as agile as swimming dragons, and their advances, retreats, fast and slow movements were all in moderation. The love songs and dances were so mesmerizing that they made people sigh with admiration. There were two bands of music, with dozens of musicians. The music was lively and melodious, and it was a good performance by Shanghai's most famous Causanova band. The listeners could not help but clap their hands. The shawls, treasure fans, and bone combs needed for the Spanish dance were all provided by Mrs. Keyinhan of Yousheng Social Club, which were antique and extremely valuable. It is said that tonight is the last day, and the audience will be even more crowded.

Conspiracy to Murder

▲ Liu Youlong and others taken into custody separately

The gangster Liu Youlong, nicknamed "Pockmarked Long," on the afternoon of the first of this month, gathered his gang members Cao Shunchu (aka Little Cao), Sun Asi, Zhu Tianfu, Jiang Shaosheng, Li Agen, Lu Asan, Zhou Gensheng, Ai Ashun, Ge Acai, etc., each wielding sharp axes and handguns, and went to the Dafang Stack entrance on Min'guo Road, Fujian Road, in the French Concession, intending to seek revenge on Sun Zhongmou. Fortunately, Sun saw the situation was unfavorable and immediately fled into the Chinese territory. Liu and others were about to pursue him when they were intercepted by French Concession detectives Chen Sanlin, patrol officers Mao Jinsheng, Lu Jinchen, Bao Tan Gu Mingzhou, Jiang Changwen, etc. They stepped forward, apprehended Liu and the others one after another, confiscated the sharp axes and weapons, and took them to the police station. Yesterday, they were brought before the French court for investigation.

First, Sun Zhongmou testified, stating that he was twenty-one years old and worked as a runner at the Trading Company at 567 Shanxi Road. On September 30th, the merchant encountered Liu Youlong at Xiaodongmen. Liu immediately accused the merchant of having an affair with his teacher's wife and forcefully demanded a loan of 300 yuan. The merchant refused because it was untrue. Liu then threatened him, saying that if he didn't lend the money, he would use an axe against him. The merchant ignored him and they parted ways. Unexpectedly, at 3 PM on October 1st, the merchant was walking from the Chinese territory to the entrance of Dafang Stack at Xiaodongmen when he saw Liu leading more than ten people, intending to provoke him. As a result, the merchant fled into the Chinese territory, fortunately protected by the police, and was not harmed. Otherwise, he would have been murdered. Now that they have been arrested, he requests a thorough investigation.

Questioned, Liu Youlong confessed that he was twenty-five years old, from Ningbo, and used to work at a laundry. After losing his job, he associated with gangsters and worshipped Han Ahu, also known as "Woof Woof" Ahu, as his "old man." It was because Sun Zhongmou had an affair with his teacher's wife, Lao Qi, the wife of Han Ahu. After he discovered this, Sun initially agreed to pay him 300 yuan as compensation. Unexpectedly, Sun not only failed to pay but also gathered many people to beat him. Therefore, he harbored resentment and gathered his brothers on this day, hoping to murder Sun.

Cao Shunchu and others testified similarly, confirming that they were indeed invited by "Pockmarked" Long to assist in the crime. The Chinese and Western judges sentenced Liu Youlong to 18 months in the Western prison, Cao Shunchu, Sun Asi, and Zhu Afu to one year each, and Li Agen, Jiang Shaosheng, and the other six to nine months each. Upon completion of their sentences, they will all be permanently expelled from the Concession. The confiscated axes were confiscated.

Verification of the Death of a Prisoner

Jin Hengcan, a local, forty-one years old, worked as an accountant in the Customs Department of Jardine Matheson in the New Yong'an Street of the French Concession. This spring, he was accused in the French court of privately opening iron boxes and embezzling a huge sum of money. The court found him guilty and sentenced him to imprisonment, which he was serving. Recently, Jin fell ill in prison, and medical treatment was ineffective. He died on the 14th. The prison guard notified Tongren Fuyuantang, who sent laborers to carry the body to the morgue. At the same time, the police station informed the deceased's family. Yesterday, Jin Ruizhan, the son of the deceased, purchased clothing and a coffin for the body, which was transported back to his hometown for burial.

Continued Hearing of the Manslaughter Case Against the Foreman

▲Further Investigation is Required to Ascertain the Truth

Dong Dexing, a small worker from Anhui in the flannel workshop of the Ewo Yarns Mill, through a lawyer, has accused the foremen of the mill, Wang Jiekui, Wang Guofang, and Wang Jiexian, of conspiring to assault him with axes on the morning of August 6th, at 6:00 AM, with the intent to murder him, which they failed to achieve. The Special Court has already held three hearings, ordering the detention of Wang Jiekui, and requiring Wang Guofang and Wang Jiexian to each post a 1,000-yuan bail. This has already been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Cheng Shangfeng, who is in charge of this case, continued the hearing in the Fifth Criminal Court. The defendants were also represented by three lawyers, Chen Tingrui, Fan Gang, and Ding Rong. The plaintiff, Dong Dexing, repeated his previous accusations and testified that the defendant Wang Jiekui was at the scene giving commands to strike, and that he was still wearing the same clothes he wore that day. Furthermore, witnesses Zhang Songbai and Ye Xirong testified, presenting evidence. However, Ye testified that Wang Jiekui was wearing gray clothes at the time of the incident, which was greatly different from Zhang's testimony. The Western factory manager of Ewo Yarns Mill also testified, proving that the three defendants worked in the factory with good conduct and had never had any faults. Subsequently, the lawyer Chen Tingrui, representing the defendants, stated that his firm had obtained Dong Dexing's report to the Yangshupu police station from that day, signed by the police chief. The report stated that there were more than thirty assailants at the time, all unknown by name, and that the incident occurred at the intersection of Yangzhou Road and Taopeng Road. However, Dong now testifies that the incident occurred in front of No. 61, Xin Kang Li, Yangzhou Road, and that he saw Wang Jiekui commanding the assault, with a total of seven people. The testimony differs from the report and should be carefully examined. Judge Cheng reported that further investigation of the case was necessary, and postponed the hearing for seven days, issuing a subpoena for the police chief to bring the records to the court for further verification.

Sampan Operator Tragically Drowns

▲ Sailors Act Unreasonably

Xin Dingchang, a thirty-year-old man from Ningbo, operated sampan No. 130, carrying passengers for a living in the Yangshupu area. At 7 PM the night before, the sampan was docked near the Witama Road pier in Yangshupu, and then docked between buoys 10 and 13 of the Shanghai Customs Station. Two French sailors from the Chenonceaux merchant ship hailed Xin's sampan from the shore to ferry them to the ship. After the two sailors paid and boarded the ship, another French sailor on board wanted to go ashore, so he took Xin's sampan to the shore. At that time, the sampan had not yet left the ship, and another Frenchman on board also wanted to take Xin's boat to the shore. Xin agreed, asking one of the sailors to wait a moment. However, the sailor had no sense and was impatient. Without hearing Xin's explanation, the sailor grabbed Xin and started punching and kicking him. Xin was unprepared and was suddenly knocked into the river, sinking to the bottom, resulting in a tragic drowning. Seeing the trouble he caused, the sailor took another boat to shore. Later, Xin's father, Hesheng, learned of the incident. He believed that his son had died tragically and that the French sailor treated Chinese lives worse than chickens and dogs. Therefore, he went to the police station and cried out, demanding justice. He claimed that his son and he depended on operating the sampan for a living, and that the French sailor acted unreasonably and used violence. He requested an investigation. At the same time, two sampan operators, Ge Amao of No. 1156 and Zhu Gengsheng of No. 795, arrived at the police station and testified about the French sailor's actions. The police chief immediately dispatched detective Deng Jiagen to investigate the ship. He instructed Xin's father to wait for notification from the French Consulate for verification.

Year-End Accounting in the Gregorian Calendar

▲ Problems Persist Among Merchants

The year-end accounting in the Gregorian calendar this year cannot be delayed any further. However, businesses dealing in beans, rice, Southern goods, and daily necessities rely on the winter season for their annual business opportunities. The Gregorian New Year falls in mid-November of the Lunar calendar, when people buy more goods than usual, and the stores are fully stocked. If the financial community wants to settle the year's debts at this time, it would be difficult to achieve from a practical standpoint. Therefore, the rice industry once submitted a request to the Bureau of Social Affairs to forward to the Central Government, requesting accommodation, and also sent a letter to the Money Exchange Association to inform its members to allow for flexibility and postpone the year-end accounting until the end of January next year. Afterwards, the Money Exchange Association did not express its opinion, and is awaiting the government's approval.

No Further Extension for Wheat Inspection

▲ Effective October 21st

▲ Must Report to the Inspection Office According to Law

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the guilds of grain, oil cake, and beans and rice in the city yesterday, stating that the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Office of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines had informed them that the inspection of wheat for sale in Shanghai would begin on October 1st, and that goods arriving before October 1st would be registered free of charge until October 5th. Later, the Shanghai Grain, Oil Cake and Bean Industry Guild requested an extension until October 12th, which was announced. Now, representatives from the Shanghai Grain, Oil Cake and Bean Industry Guild, Ye Huijun, Cai Yukun, Zhu Yunliang, Jiang Lansheng, She Bingwen, etc., have requested another extension until October 20th, stating that registering inventory and inspecting new goods requires investigation, preparation, and complicated procedures, which are difficult to complete in a short time. This has been approved, and it has been decided that all wheat arriving in Shanghai before October 20th must be registered at the office by October 20th. From October 21st, the temporary regulations for wheat inspection must be followed, and both old and new goods transported in transit must be processed as new goods. However, after this extension, no further extensions will be granted. A corresponding letter is sent to your chamber of commerce to inform your members. The letter stated that since the deadline for free registration was requested and set by the representatives of the industries concerned, it would be difficult to extend it again. In addition to sending separate letters to the industries concerned to inform them, a corresponding letter is sent to your association to inform all members.

(1) Discussion on how to handle the case of Xu Shaochuan, a former member of the executive committee, who was not re-elected after his term expired and has not yet returned to the company. It was resolved to send a letter to withdraw. (2) It was resolved that Yu Yaoqiu will be responsible for all external affairs of the union in the future. Passed. (3) What should be done with the outstanding salary of the English professor? It was resolved to send a letter requesting it. (4) The salary increases for members Jin and Zhang have not been implemented yet. It was resolved to send another letter to the company to implement them immediately.

Fire in Western Shanghai Last Night

At around 10 PM last night, a fire suddenly broke out at a business on Connaught Road in western Shanghai. The smoke was thick and the fire lit up the sky. The fire brigade rushed to the scene upon hearing the news and extinguished the fire after some time. Statistics show that two or three city houses were destroyed.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky will be mostly cloudy with fog in the morning. Northwesterly winds will strengthen north of Shandong, while there will be northeasterly to southeasterly winds to the south. There is a low-pressure system in Jiangxi. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 80.6 degrees and the lowest was 58.4 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 72.6 degrees and the lowest was 48.6 degrees.

▲ Correction: In the report yesterday about the kidnapping suspect Gu Aqing, there was a slight error in the words of Judge Xu to the police station regarding the lawyer's statement. At that time, Judge Xu declared, "During the investigation, if exculpatory evidence favorable to the defendant is discovered, it may be brought to court for trial at any time before the scheduled date," and not that the complaint was withdrawn. This is specifically corrected.
