Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Seafarer

▲ Policeman (to a beggar): What is your name? Where do you live?

Beggar: You want to know my name and address? I am called Common People. I live at No. 1 Open Air. If you condescend to visit, there is no need to knock. Just come in.

▲ Math Teacher: Children, suppose there is a plate here, with a cake on it. I bring it in and cut it with a knife, and divide it among you to eat. Student A eats one-fifth. Student B eats one-fifth. Student C eats one-fifth. I myself eat two-fifths. How much is left?

A Student: Teacher, there is still a plate left.

▲ Mother (scolding her young daughter): You girls should know etiquette from a young age. For example, when you come down the stairs, you must be light on your feet and not make any noise. Do you understand?

Daughter: I understand. I'll go upstairs to try it now. (Goes upstairs. Returns to the room after a while.)

Mother: That was good. You came downstairs and I didn't hear a sound.

Daughter: Mother, I slid down the banister of the stairs. It was fast and there was no noise.

▲ Man: I have an important question to ask you. I have been preparing for a week.

Woman: Ask quickly. I have been preparing the answer for several months.

Excerpts from Wu Zhihui's Speech

— Jia Ming

A National Day celebration was held by West Lake. No fewer than 50,000 people from various agencies, schools, and factories participated. The weather that day was bright and cheerful. A solemn and enthusiastic atmosphere filled the entire venue. In addition to Central Committee members Chen Guofu and Cheng Jian, and Department Heads Zhou Cai and other executive members of the Party headquarters, Mr. Wu Zhihui, who named the "Double Tenth Festival," also arrived after attending a provincial government meeting in car number seven. Wu was bald and wore a Yuan-style mandarin jacket made of woolen fabric. When he took the stage, photographers scrambled to take pictures. Wu stood up and smiled in response. He sometimes looked at promotional materials, using his old-fashioned copper-rimmed reading glasses. His simplicity was evident. He stood up to give a speech amidst applause from thousands of people, blending solemnity and humor, with words that were exceptionally wonderful. I noted them down to enrich this discussion.

▲ Top-Quality Imported Goods

Sixty years ago, Chinese people were always startled when they saw blue-eyed foreigners. Everyone praised and admired those who had straight legs, white skin, and looked like monkeys. Because they were imported goods, because they were top-quality imported goods.

▲ Fighting for the Honor of Yellow Faces

China had Yao, Shun, and the Yellow Emperor six thousand years ago. Which country in the world can compare? Most countries didn't have scholars until the time of Confucius. Although Egyptian civilization was also early, look at their wall paintings, what are they like? The Three Principles of the People were invented by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. It can be said to be the best in the world, and it can also be said to be the crystallization of six thousand years of thought. Because of Mr. Sun Yat-sen, we can fight for the honor of yellow faces.

▲ Writing an Insurance Policy

The applicability of Mr. Sun Yat-sen's principles is suitable for at least a thousand years. If I were to write an insurance policy like in a clock shop, I would boldly write a guarantee for a thousand years without hesitation.

▲ What is Marx?

Marxism, Niu Marxism, causing a chaotic mess. The theory is not worth refuting. It's just because he was born fifty years earlier, so what he saw and heard was not as profound as Mr. Sun Yat-sen. He took the wrong path, just like I wrote stereotyped essays for thirty years.

▲ Zhang Fei and Niu Gao Represent Black People

We shouldn't only say that white people are good. Who knows if black people will dominate in the future? Our ancient Zhang Fei and Niu Gao were all black-faced.

▲ The Premier's Will Includes the Entire Constitution

Speaking of political tutelage, let me give an example: Yi Yin assisting Tai Jia, the Duke of Zhou assisting King Cheng. Mr. Sun Yat-sen said that 400 million people are the emperor, which is also A Dou. Now, the period of political tutelage is necessary for 400 million emperors to understand the Three Principles of the People and to establish a constitution when the National Assembly is convened to govern the Republic of China. In fact, a constitution is not just any provisional law, it is already included in the Premier's will.

Zhongda Confers Honorary Doctorates on Foreigners Fan and Lin, a Grand Event

— Xie Fei

▲ A Zhongda Initiative

National Central University has conferred honorary doctorates on Mr. Fandewen from Belgium and Mr. Lin Baike from the United States. Both men have come to Nanjing and possess profound academic knowledge and extensive writings, making many contributions to world culture. They are especially enthusiastic about supporting our country's abolition of unequal treaties and our Party's Three Principles of the People, doing their best to promote them. Therefore, following the precedents of universities around the world, Mr. Fandewen was awarded an honorary Doctor of Literature degree, and Mr. Lin Baike was awarded an honorary Doctor of Laws degree. This was specially approved by the University Affairs Council in advance, and a committee was organized to handle the doctorate conferment ceremony. It is an unprecedented initiative.

▲ A Tall Decorated Archway

The certificate presentation ceremony was held in the university gymnasium at 5:00 PM on the 9th of this month. As the next day was National Day, the decorations were extremely splendid. Outside the school gate, a tall decorated archway was erected, with the words "National Central University Confers Honorary Doctorates on Fandewen and Lin Baike." Inside the gate, the path leading to the gymnasium was very wide. In the shade of willows and tung trees, Party and national flags and red lanterns congratulating National Day were countless. When the day passed, thousands of red stars could be seen, rippling in the moonlight like water, giving people a sense of freshness.

▲ Arriving Late

After 3:00 PM, attendees arrived one after another. By 4:30 PM, the upper level was full, and later arrivals were still like a tide. However, after repeated delays and anticipation, the two doctors finally appeared on the red and green floral altar at 5:30 PM amidst thunderous applause.

▲ A Talented President

Before the certificates were presented, President Zhang Naiyan gave a report, roughly as described in the first paragraph. First in Chinese, then in French, and then in English, because French is used in Belgium and English in the United States.

▲ Mr. Fandewen's Speech

Mr. Fandewen also gave a speech titled "International Economic Relations." He said that in modern times, due to convenient transportation, international relations have arisen. China used to be closed and self-sufficient, but was broken down by foreigners, hence the movement to recover tariffs and achieve autonomy today. I sincerely hope it can be realized soon. Recently, France advocated the so-called European Federation issue, but it must start with economic union, which is hopeless given today's environment. European economy can be divided into two sides: one agricultural, one industrial. Politics also differs accordingly. Eastern Europe is the world of manpower and animal power, while Western Europe is the world of motors. The latter uses coal and machinery, the former uses manpower and animal power. Their evolution is different, and their strength is different. Only the world that uses motors relies on force and technology as a backing. The former, that is, the agricultural countries of other continents, can rise up and advance, countering each other, and can also apply electricity to agricultural improvements, avoiding the mistakes of Europe and the United States, and avoiding the errors of imperialism. His inventions are a blessing for the whole world, and true peace can be realized.

▲ Mr. Lin's Speech

Mr. Lin said that he was deeply touched by Mr. Fandewen's speech. He believed that there are only three countries in the world that are self-sufficient: China, the United States, and Russia. China has vast land and abundant resources, like a world of its own, and can survive on its own. It is only because of foreign constraints that it cannot be free. Recently, the people of China have been working hard on this and have become more aware. Those in power are especially eager to develop Chinese industries, which is very promising. He also said that seeking knowledge is to obtain true happiness. Knowledge that is not harmonious and fluid is not true knowledge. Like Mr. Sun Yat-sen, it is not just for knowledge, but for the happiness of all. Before and after his speech, he respectfully bowed three times to the portrait of the Premier.

▲ Our Way is Western

Mr. Lou Tongsun, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, said: "Mr. Fandewen and Mr. Lin each hold a diploma to return with, which is like holding a flag of our country. Our way is Western. Both gentlemen are of high moral character and respected, and their scholarship shakes China and foreign countries. Today, they receive this honor, which is well deserved. I sincerely hope that in thirty years, there will be two people in the audience today who will each seize a flag and return."

Thinking of Western Medicine from National Products

— Cocoa

Recently, Shanghai is holding a national products movement. National products, national products, the words fill the ears. I think that there are more and more national products for daily use. All citizens should use them as much as possible. However, the overseas imports of medical and pharmaceutical products are increasing year by year. Especially various over-the-counter medicines. They are convenient to take and sell in large quantities. Just conduct a brief survey of the market and you will find it hard to list them all. Although medicine has no national boundaries, considering the huge amount of leakage, we should be disheartened. It is advisable to expect those with aspirations in the pharmaceutical industry to work hard to create and produce them, so that they can meet the needs of our people. Fortunately, in recent years, pharmacies have been doing some research and gradually producing products. For example, there are Weitamins 54 and other brands of beef juice. For cod liver oil emulsion, there are Jiufu, Jiuxing, and other brands. There are even more brands of malt extract. There is also a kind of Yar's preparation, which is made from the essence of cod liver oil, without its fishy taste. It has always been popular among the intellectual class, and is favored by those who are weak, coughing, and in the early stages of lung disease. It used to be an imported product only, and the annual sales are alarming. Recently, there is also a considerable amount of national product, namely the so-called Bulito. All of these are only a small part of over-the-counter medicines, but I hope to progress and develop day by day from this. From two or three kinds to hundreds of kinds. From small parts to large parts. And from over-the-counter medicines to raw materials. It is hoped that in the future, all medical treatment will not need to be sought abroad. This can be called the ultimate goal of promotion. The gentlemen in the pharmaceutical industry should strive for it.

Italian Art Study Notes (4)

— Wang Yachen

(4) The Pitti Palace. Palace Pitti is in Florence, west of the beautiful Arno River. It is surrounded by a wide square. The palace is located on the plateau of the square. It was originally a royal palace built with huge stones. It is surrounded by woods. Looking from the plateau, you can see the distant scenery outside the city. This is one of the grand palaces in Florence. It was built in 1444. From 1550 to 1895, it was the private residence of the Duke of Tuscany. Although it is now an art gallery, it is still owned by the royal family. Entering the gallery, go straight to the third floor. From the first room to the sixth room, there are large murals. The decorations when the Duke lived there are still preserved. The interior is exquisite, with incredible painted beams and carved pillars. Each mural is different. Looking up at the stone pillars painted on the ceiling, connected to the buildings below, they look like real objects, difficult to distinguish. Italian murals are famous in the world, especially the murals in palaces and aristocratic residences, all of which are masterpieces by famous artists of the time, making us linger. The gallery displays not only Italian masterpieces, but also more than twenty masterpieces from the Netherlands and Spain.

Painting in Spain and the Netherlands in the seventeenth century was very distinctive. But they all accepted the style of the High Renaissance and continued to inspire it. Morillo of Spain and Rubens of the Netherlands both studied in Florence. Their skills advanced rapidly, surpassing those of Italy at the time. Now, the works of Spain and the Netherlands are displayed in this gallery, all of which are collections from the palace in the past, and are extremely precious.

There are more antiques in this gallery, and also many paintings, but not as complete as the Uffizi Gallery. The two major galleries in Florence are the Uffizi and the Pitti. The other masterpieces are scattered in various churches. To study Italian painting and sculpture, in addition to the two galleries, one must also explore the murals of various temples to see their full extent.

(5) The Church of Santa Croce. St. Croce The church is located in the city of Florence. In front of it is a large open space. In the middle of the space stands a stone statue of the poetic saint Dante, more than ten feet high. This statue is a work by Michelangelo. The expression of Dante is carved to perfection. Below the statue is a stone platform with four lions. The shape of the lions is not carved according to nature, but has a style of ancient Greece. To the right of the church, there is another ancient temple. It displays a large mural by Giotto Giollo. Below depicts "The Last Supper." Above depicts "The Ascension of Jesus." This painting is very precious in history. Tickets must be purchased to enter here, which is different from other places.

European Travelogue (79)

— Liu Haisu

▲ Diary of Touring Italy

(3) Ten Days in Rome (2)

— The Eternal City — La Ville eternelle

June 1 — Spanish Masterpiece Exhibition and Japanese Modern Art Exhibition

The roads in Rome are winding and circuitous due to the high and low terrain of the hills and the avoidance of many historical sites. They are completely different from the straight avenues of Paris. However, what is easiest to feel is that the stone pillars and sculptures in the squares and even the decorations on the fountains in Paris clearly imitate the relics of ancient Rome, but they just enlarge the form. That's how it is. Even the famous Arc de Triomphe of Napoleon in Paris is just an enlarged model of the Roman style.

The architecture of the new art gallery is also very magnificent. This imitation-classical stone building is decorated with light reliefs on both sides. We stepped into it from dozens of majestic stone steps. In front of the door are many huge stone pillars. A banner of the Spanish Masterpiece Exhibition is hung in the center. It is very solemn and eye-catching. The names ElGreco, Goya, Velazquez, Zurbaran Murillo, De Ribera, Lopez, Lucas, and Carducho are written on the banner. With a satisfied smile, I calmly walked into the second door. I saw huge sculptures displayed in the inner courtyard. It was already enough to make us praise. Walking straight to the left, it was the Spanish exhibition. Walking inside, I saw the famous masterpiece "The Tears of St. Peter" by El Creco, which I had seen in prints. Most of this room is filled with El Greco's masterpieces. Further on are the paintings of Velazquez and Murillo. Further in are the paintings of Bayeu Carducho Ribera and Goya. Finally, there are the paintings of Lopez Lucas and Zubaran. The total number of paintings is sixty-six. Ten by El Greco, four by Murillo, seven by Velazquez, four by Ribera, seven by Goya. The rest I don't remember clearly. It was an unexpected pleasure for me to see so many masterpieces of Spanish masters in Rome. Although I knew about the Spanish school of painting before and liked the paintings of El Greco and Goya, I never had a thorough understanding of them. Now I have realized the true meaning of these masterpieces. Especially after reading their history and biographies, I imagined their works as being full of rich vitality. However, it is futile to have no chance to see the works in person. Now I have seen them all. It is what I understand and appreciate. This can be considered the first happy event in my life.

Financial and Gold Markets Turn Downward

▲ Exhausting the Art of Change

Yesterday, the 17th, the gold market suddenly turned downward. However, the situation was volatile, sometimes high, sometimes low, unstoppable. In the morning, there were two or three taels of fluctuations. In the afternoon, it seemed peaceful, hovering only by one or two taels. In short, people's hearts were unsettled, and the market was agitated to fall. There were a total of four taels and three mace of review throughout the day. Foreign exchange seemed loose. Banks all had deposits and withdrawals. The market transactions were divergent. In the previous session, large firms such as Yuan Mao Yong Zhi Feng Yong Fu Yu Shun Li Wan Xing, and arbitrageurs, mostly bought in. Sellers included Heng Xing Yong Kang Yuan Tai Xie Yu, etc. It showed weakness from the early market. The overseas silver market was still. The silver price rose instead. Because yesterday's expectation of a drop did not materialize. The European market was extremely flat. Citibank had no intention to buy or sell. The gold price failed to support itself. Soon after, it broke the 560 tael mark. Buyers showed courage and arbitrageurs chased the price. At noon, it re-entered the mark. The atmosphere in the market improved as the banks took in British gold. It soared to 64 taels. In the afternoon, Cheng Feng Yong Shun Li Fu Chang and Wupin had already bought, while Heng Xing Tai Xing, etc., still sold. It was stable at first, but then the sellers became active, and it turned lower. However, there were still signs of accumulation. Finally, it was calculated at 61 taels and change.

Long-Term Interest Rate Opens at 9.5%

▲Pawnshops at 8.5%

The long-term funds that are due this time are not dared to be relaxed due to various reasons, so there are no large transactions even after a long time. It is found that the recent interest rates for long-term funds in the silver and money industry are sparse. The large-scale transactions in the market have not yet started. In the past two days, it was heard that the financial sector has made a few regulations on the due transfer funds of Shenxin, Fuxin, and the three factories, and the interest rate is still 9.5%, which is comparable to the price in April. In addition, pawnshops have made a few, and the interest rate is 8.5%. Most of the wholesale businesses in the foreign firm street area and most of the large stores have not made regulations. According to people in the financial industry, the funding for this long-term loan is one-third more than the first half of the year, and there are no suitable borrowers for a while, so they have to wait and see the opportunity. As for the level of interest rates, it is difficult to be opportunistic in the current dilemma.

The Cotton Yarn Market Returns to a Soft State

At the same time, spot yarn sales are increasingly deserted, so the market sentiment is trending downward again. However, manufacturers are still entering, so the market has not yet seen a major fall.

The Starch Market Is Fraught with Peril

▲Major Decline Slightly Recovered: Steady Outlook

Yesterday's starch market experienced a major turbulence during the opening session in the morning, as the price of foreign wheat fell by another 6-7 cents. With the gradual decline in spot wheat from foreign countries, the mentality of all parties has changed. Not only are the inland bulls extremely panicked, but also the factories are almost unanimously inclined to sell out. Due to the massive reverse sales by the bulls during the opening session, the market price plummeted and could not be salvaged. The lowest price for this month was 2.22 yuan, 2.18 yuan for November, 2.1975 yuan for December and January, 2.2075 yuan for February, and 2.215 yuan for March, a sharp drop of 3-4-5 points compared with the closing price of the previous day. However, after the second session, the bulls took the opportunity to replenish their positions due to the excessive decline, so the market also rebounded strongly. When the afternoon session opened, the market sentiment had become stable due to the major decline and small rebound, and there were not many ups and downs in each month. Looking at the steady outlook, there is really no reason to fall further to this point, and it should be temporarily circling. As a result, this month was down by 1.25 cents compared to the previous day, November and December were down by 1 cent, January and February were down by 0.25 cents, and March was unchanged.

Futures and Spot Wheat Both Plummet Again

▲The Decline in the Evening Market Comes to an End

Yesterday's futures wheat market saw the softness of the mentality reaching its peak after the opening session in the morning. Since foreign wheat has been ordered by factories, and the sale of spot wheat is also constantly on the way, the trend of wheat will of course be softened by foreign countries. Therefore, the bulls in the near and far terms have reached this environment and can no longer fight like trapped beasts. They can only take advantage of the trend to close out. Due to the competition among bulls, the market could not be salvaged. For example, the lowest price for November was 4.24 yuan, and the price for December was 4.22 yuan, which is similar to the standard of new wheat. The prices for January, February, and March also fell to 4.26 yuan, and it was seen that the situation was not good at that time, with the wheat not being worth much. When the afternoon session opened, the market rebounded slightly due to the slight recovery in the starch market and the competition among shorts. However, it was still slightly lower than the closing price of the previous day. As a result, October and November fell by 4 cents, December fell by 3 cents, and January, February, and March fell by 4 cents. The spot wheat market also saw a sharp decline, which was even worse in the middle and second grades. The lowest price was 4.00 yuan to enter customs, which was as low as 8 cents. It is said that more than 4,000 bags of wheat from Dongtai and Gaoyou were opened in the city's Guandian and handled by Xinda.

Rice Market

Hu Nan (Southern Shanghai)

Yesterday, 32 to 33 boats from the southern head gangs arrived. Market sales were extremely sluggish. White粳 rice prices fell by half a yuan. Yang Du Jian rice was also lower by 1 to 2 jiao. The remaining goods were offered loosely.

Zhabei (Northern Shanghai)

Yesterday, over 50 boats arrived from upstream. The market appetite was very weak. New 粳 rice prices fell sharply by 5 to 6 jiao. Yang Jian, Du Jian, Yin Bian Yuan, etc., fell by 3 jiao. The rest were down by 2 jiao. Only the top Bo Dao rice, with limited stock, had stable prices.

Shanghai Market

Market News

▲The Dongyulun Silk and Satin Shop on Wangping Street, Nanjing Road, declares: "Our shop's aim is to serve society. Our selection of goods and pricing are unique and outstanding. Since opening, business has been thriving and our reputation has been growing. While honored, we dare not be complacent. We strive to serve and continuously improve, always focusing on quality and low prices, and always aiming for customer satisfaction. To reciprocate the patronage of all sectors, we will hold an autumn sale for 30 days starting October 12th. Every Sunday, we will also offer a complimentary genuine silk handkerchief."

▲The Huangjiuzhitang Pharmacy on Zhejiang Road declares: "Since our opening on August 16th, a full month has passed in the blink of an eye. Due to low prices and quality goods, our doors are crowded daily. Ginseng, bird's nest, fine medicines, and prepared slices and powders are all selling briskly. Among the pills and powders, Ginseng Rejuvenation Pills are particularly popular and are the top seller. During the first month of our opening, we offered a 30% discount to attract customers. Now that the first month is over, to continue to benefit our customers, we will continue to offer discounts. Our original plan was a 10% discount on weekdays and a 9.1% discount on the 1st, 15th, and Sundays. Now, during the continued discount period, we will offer a 9.1% discount every day. If the 1st, 15th, or a Sunday falls within this period, we will offer an additional 5% discount on top of the 9.1% discount, which is almost the same as the 30% discount offered during the first month of opening."

▲The Zhongqihua Company on Nanjing Road declares: "Our piece goods department has recently received a large shipment of fashionable women's overcoat velvet, all-wool men's and women's overcoat velvet, western-style suiting fabric, trendy patterned velvet, autumn overcoat wool, new patterned woolen crepe, window and door bunting, curtain fabric, new striped camel wool, patterned lining velvet, etc. During the current discount period, we are genuinely sacrificing profits and selling at cost. Customers are flocking to our store, demonstrating the low prices."

▲The Wangshuntai Woolen Fabric and Western Clothing Shop, opposite Lloyd Road on Nanjing Road, declares: "We have recently received a large shipment of unique patterned woolen fabrics, parti-colored bunting, and overcoat and robe materials, which have all arrived in succession. Therefore, starting yesterday, we are holding an autumn sale for 30 days. These goods are most suitable for making Western suits, with bright and beautiful colors and a unique aesthetic. Moreover, the prices are particularly low, so customers are flocking to order them, and business is very crowded."

▲The Liede'er Restaurant at 157-159 Avenue Dubail declares: "After several months of preparation, we are officially opening today. We offer exquisite Western cuisine at very reasonable prices. In the evenings, Western women will perform Western plays from 10:00 PM to 6:00 AM the next morning. In order to benefit Chinese ladies, there will be no admission fee."

▲The Taifeng Canned Food Company on Nanjing Road declares: "Our company has a long-standing reputation for snacks. A few months ago, we hired a Cantonese pastry chef who has special skills in snack preparation. Recently, this pastry chef has created three new types of pastries: lotus seed paste puff dumplings, red bean paste puff dumplings, and egg yolk puff balls. Their color, aroma, and taste are excellent and have a unique flavor. In recent days, these three products have been so popular that we can barely keep up with demand. The skillful cooking and the public's welcome are evident."

▲The Hanli Company declares: "Since our newly invented Zhongling Printing Machine was promoted by the Ministers of Education, Industry, Commerce, Railways, and Interior of Nanjing, people from all walks of life have recognized the importance of the machine and have been purchasing it in a continuous stream. Agents from various provinces and foreign countries have also been vying to place orders. Our company has also recently released a new edition of the Chinese Economical Telegraph Code. This book was compiled by Tan Rongguang, a famous scholar from Guangdong Province. The words and phrases are well-connected and all-encompassing. It has the same function as the Bentheny's English code, which is sold worldwide. Major commercial firms can use this code to transmit messages, saving two-thirds of their telegraph costs. The code uses a group of three English letters to represent a Chinese character, a company name, a place name, an idiom, or a secret agreement. Three groups are combined and an additional guarantee letter is added, making a total of ten letters per sentence. The telegraph office charges only one character's fee, but it can convey the meaning of three characters, achieving the effectiveness of dozens of characters. The code is particularly detailed in collecting information for the banking and shipping industries, and it is even more practical for overseas Chinese trade. Having this code is a great benefit for businesses, and it has been purchased by many. Our company's business in both areas has been very prosperous recently."

▲The Yongan Hosiery Factory declares: "Our owner has decades of experience and has built a Western-style market house on Dongmen Road outside Xiaodongmen, with a large clock embedded in the door for the convenience of pedestrians. The factory has purchased a wide range of machinery to produce various kinds of silk, yarn, and velvet socks. Among them, the economical socks are inexpensive and of good quality, and are very popular with the public. All purchases of one yuan or more will receive a full set of the Lingbo Qianying movie clips as a thank you for your patronage. The grand opening was on the 17th."

▲The Sino-French Clock and Watch Shop declares: "Yesterday was the first day of our grand opening, and patronage from all sectors was exceptionally enthusiastic because our prices are indeed fair. Many number 6 rectangular gold-filled watches were sold. The main distribution point is located at the French Concession Avenue Mash Street entrance to the automatic fire road."

▲The China Weiyi Woolen Fabric Factory declares: "Since establishing our main distribution point at 51 Niuzhuang Road, our business has greatly flourished because our Double Deer brand camel wool products are becoming increasingly refined and the patterns are even more novel. It is also convenient for customers to wholesale, and all ordered goods can be delivered daily, which is very convenient. Recently, we have been very busy and somewhat overwhelmed. Our newly installed telephone number is 17016."

▲The Yonghua Company Department Store, located at the intersection of Rue de Consulat and West Xinqiao Street, declares: "Our store specializes in selling various global goods and is organized with great care. As soon as our new building is completed, we will select an auspicious day for the grand opening."

Theater News

▲The Paris Grand Theater declares: "Starting today, we will be screening the tragic war epic, Blood and Tears. The film stars Janet Gaynor and Charles Farrell and features a dramatic and moving storyline. Our theater has recently installed a new sound system that plays special music to accompany the film. In addition to the dialogue, all other sounds are clearly transmitted, making the audience feel as if they are in a talking picture theater, without the barrier of language."

▲The Central Grand Theater declares: "Starting today, we will be screening the martial arts and romance epic, Adventure in the Bandit's Den. This film is the latest production from the Yueming Company and features many exciting and interesting plot twists, such as a female thief turning against her comrades, a night raid on the bandit's den, a rivalry between female thieves for the bandit's affection, and a group of bandits acting foolishly. It is both lively and entertaining and is truly a masterpiece of Chinese cinema."

▲The Wuchang Grand Theater declares: "Starting today, our theater will be screening Charlie Chaplin's comedy, The Four Convicts, and The Kid, starring Little Huzi. The slapstick comedy will have audiences in stitches."

▲The World Grand Theater at the corner of Qingyun Road in Zhabei declares: "Starting today, we will be screening the martial arts and adventure film, Jiangnan Female Knight, day and night. This film is the latest production from the Great Wall Film Company and features a dramatic and compelling storyline that is in line with modern trends. It depicts heroic qualities and warns against unscrupulous gentry. The main roles are played by Qian Siying and Wang Zhengqing, and it is directed by Yang Xiaozhong, adding even more luster to the film. It is a leading work in the genre of domestic martial arts films."

Youth Corner

Impressions of a Northern Tour

— Su Ling

(14) Northern Mountain Temple Fair and Singing Girls

During the last three days of our trip, we happened to coincide with the date of the temple fair that the citizens of Jilin city were passionately gathering for, seemingly devoutly. (Probably the Buddha bathing festival, but I didn't inquire in detail, not knowing if the bodhisattva in the temple was a Buddha or a deity.) This was also the event that the students considered to be the most exciting.

It was indeed very lively. Rickshaws (i.e., Huang Bao cars), horse-drawn carriages, and crowds of people clogged the narrow roads, even though Northern Mountain was still far away.

Although Northern Mountain wasn't as desolate as a wilderness on ordinary days, visitors were always rare. However, during the temple fair, people were as crowded as ants gathering on a piece of food, packed on and off the mountain.

Well in advance, many merchants had set up market stalls from the foot of the mountain to the mountainside. Among these, the most numerous were teahouses selling cold and hot drinks, and every teahouse was filled with visitors.

We mixed into the crowd and climbed up the mountain.

These people, women, men, old, young… Among them, girls wearing fashionable clothes were in the minority (among this minority, most were prostitutes). From this, we can see that Jilin is still a simple and unsophisticated ancient city.

Upon arriving at a temple halfway up the mountain, it was filled with smoke, and I really couldn't get used to breathing inside. Most of the women who came to the mountain would come to the temple to burn incense and kowtow a few times, but most of the men came to watch the excitement, the so-called "strolling the temple fair," as we were doing.

There were also many amusement venues on and off the mountain: magic shows by Japanese and Koreans, stereoscopes (i.e., looking at picture slides), Peking opera stages, and teahouses where storytelling with drum accompaniment was performed. We found a teahouse with drum storytelling and went in to rest and relax.

I vaguely remember seeing drum storytelling once in Shanghai at the Great World or the Sun Sun Amusement Park. This time, I could truly experience the music and literature of the northern people, although I had no way of understanding what they were singing.

After a young singing girl finished performing, another young singing girl walked onto the stage. With one hand, she held three pieces of wood slightly apart, and with the other, she delicately held a chopstick. Bang, bang, bang, she began to strike the small drum and shake the clappers—bang, bang, bang, thump… Then, the old qin player with nearsighted eyes, wearing copper thimbles on his fingers, plucked the qin strings. Then, from between the singing girl's red lips and white teeth burst a vibrating and steady voice, like singing, but also like recounting.

When she struck the small drum for the first time, I almost jumped in surprise. This singing girl was perhaps different from the others, although she was probably even younger than them. But after that first forceful strike of the small drum, the old qin player seemed to pluck the qin strings even more energetically, and her singing voice was equally forceful, loud, and steady. She was able to quiet the clamor in the audience.

…Bang, bang, bang, bang, bang… This nervous singing girl's small drum was also nervous—thumping, thumping…

Lively, noisy, crowded, chaotic… All the way until the sun set in the west, and the colored clouds in the sky reflected on the mountain peak, turning into a golden glow, did the crowds on the mountain begin to thin out. Especially the women had to go home to prepare the evening meal.

We came when the incense began to burn in the incense burner, and only went back when the incense burner only emitted the smoke of remaining ashes.

Autumn Rain Night

— Shao Zhen

(Part 1)

Rong has indeed been very busy these past few months. Not to mention that the word "busy" has reduced his sleeping and eating time by a third, even the few sparse whiskers on his chin and around his lips, which have grown almost an inch long, have had no chance to be shaved. As soon as he gets out of bed in the morning, he takes a rickshaw to the office. He always comes home between seven and eight in the evening, rarely around six in the evening. Even on Sundays, he never sits at home for an hour. For lunch, he supposedly eats some snacks very casually, sometimes even without snacks, and waits until he gets home at night to eat two meals together, consuming two bowls of rice. After finishing dinner, he picks up his pen again and writes frantically on grid paper under the electric light. He never stops writing until two o'clock, and even when he stops, he smokes a cigarette while pondering the topic for the second night's writing. Sometimes, when he gets excited, he grabs the topic, picks up his pen, and writes until dawn. Perhaps he is exhausted and fatigued, so he drops the pen, yawns twice, and collapses onto the bed. Our sweet time after marriage has been wasted by him like this, which is really unfair. As for him, his already thin face has become even more sallow this past month. Fortunately, his spirits are still good. Although he is much thinner, his attitude remains as silent, gentle, and unexpressive of fatigue as usual. However, I always worry that if he continues to work like this, it will eventually cause great harm to his body. Every night, as usual, I repeatedly advise him to rest early and leave unfinished work for tomorrow. Unfortunately, Rong, who never listens to advice, completely ignores what I say as if it were mosquitoes buzzing in his ears. I have sulked because of his stubbornness, and I have also returned to my mother's house because of his stubbornness. But, ah, what good does this do us? Later, I simply joined him in his busyness. It can also be said that I always assist him from the side every night. However, I, who failed to finish my studies, what can I do to assist him? I only help him to transcribe his drafts. However, these things are already extremely strenuous for me.

What Rong writes at home every night is entirely about the literary and artistic movement of nationalism. There are novels, essays, and plays. Regarding the literary and artistic movement of nationalism, Rong once said to me:

"Judging from the current situation, the Chinese nation can be said to be numb to the extreme. To make them all understand the consciousness of the nation is not an easy thing in itself. But the mission borne by those in the nationalist literary movement is given by the times, to lead the entire Chinese nation through the current crisis, to avoid all kinds of suffering among the nations and to elevate the entire nation to a strong position. The mission is so great, the responsibility is also so great. Those in the nationalist literary movement cannot think that this is a very difficult work and fail to take on the mission and responsibility, or hesitate and dare not go forward. They should unite with comrades on the battle line, embrace a spirit of great selflessness, and strive forward. Their striving forward is certainly with a goal, which is to sacrifice themselves for the self-determination of the entire nation. Sacrifice, sacrifice, personal sacrifice, is not a shameful thing in itself, but it is necessary to estimate how much glory this sacrifice has in the nation. By inheritance, in tradition, every Chinese is determined to uphold a principle: to be beasts of burden for their descendants. Therefore, the harm it has caused is that, even now, the Chinese are still like a pile of loose sand, like in the previous century. The literary and artistic practitioners of nationalism, in spirit, in effort, in consciousness, of course, will extract and completely eliminate this evil thought from everyone's minds and replace it with a national consciousness. As for the efforts of this group of people, of course, they will expand their spirit of great fearlessness to seek welfare for the entire nation. Welfare, the welfare of the entire nation, in today's situation, is naturally in a very distant place, perhaps in a place they want to get to but cannot see. But 'doing it is not difficult, just keep striving forward, and that place will be easily reached.' Therefore, they knew and saw that there was a crisis at hand and did not think it was a crisis. It was precisely because they knew and saw that there was a crisis at hand that they wanted to wade through the crisis for the future self-determination of the entire nation. From that day on, they shouted and stepped towards this crisis. Their stepping towards this crisis was to trample it into a broad and smooth road for the entire nation following behind to walk on safely. This is the center of their group's efforts. Now, they have already stepped on it, and they have already flattened half of this crisis. Since their work began, although their entire success, so to speak, is not today but in the future, they have already sown many seeds of national consciousness among the nation. This is truly the vitality of the entire Chinese nation, and it is truly the most fortunate thing for the entire Chinese nation.

"Speaking of literature and art again, it was originally produced from the state of consciousness formed on the national standpoint. There is no literature and art that can be produced without this. Unfortunately, China has had this kind of so-called literature and art, which has led to Chinese literature and art entering such a decadent period today. Necessarily, it has become the current crisis facing the entire Chinese nation today. The reason for this is that thought has lost its center, and culture has no way out. What is the center of thought, and what is the way out for culture? In a word, nationalism only. (To be continued)"
